Recent News of the Floods in Hubei Province 65

Relief Teams Depart to Various Counties to Aid Refugees

Bridge Completion in Hankou, Drainage Being Planned

Hankou Correspondence: This time, the floods in Wuhan have spread throughout the province. The extent of the disaster area and the number of victims have surpassed previous records. Although the water level has receded slightly, the suffering of the people remains. The urgent tasks are to provide relief, prevent epidemics, and restore transportation. It is not yet time to discuss post-disaster recovery extravagantly. The Hubei branch of the National Government Relief Committee for Flood Disasters is aware of this, so the current work is focused on addressing the immediate symptoms. For example, in terms of relief, in addition to accommodating as many refugees as possible in Wuhan and providing food and clothing, the severity of the disaster in each county is assessed separately for relief efforts. In addition, Yang Zigong, the chairman of the Northeast Four Provinces Charitable Federation, organized a relief team. The first team, led by Yang, departed for Xindi on the 7th. The second team departed for Fankou on the 8th. Both teams used large barges to transport large quantities of white rice, flour, medicines, etc., which were distributed on the spot. The remaining counties will be handled in order. In terms of epidemic prevention, Wuhan is still mainly handled by the office in Hubei established by the Central Health Administration. The outer counties are handled by the disaster relief branch, which sends personnel to assist. The branch is divided into three sections: one is the medical section, which handles the affairs of temporary hospitals, hospitals for serious illnesses, and treatment centers in various shelters; the second is the epidemic prevention section, which handles inspection affairs, nutritional diseases, and vaccinations; and the third is the sanitation engineering team, which handles cleaning and sanitation, water purification, and food inspection. Another large health team is organized to step up work separately. Currently, many refugees in Wuhan are infected with diseases, most commonly typhoid fever, dysentery, and malaria. The most deaths are among children. However, cholera and acute infectious diseases have not yet been found, perhaps due to the clear effects of epidemic prevention work. In terms of transportation, the areas outside the county that were flooded are still a vast expanse of water, making it impossible to restore transportation for the time being. However, Hankou, where the essence is concentrated, must be planned first. The first step is to build a bridge, which was completed on the 7th. The area from Hubei Street to Zhongshan Road is now passable. The long bridge lying on the waves, the complex road traversing the sky, is indeed a fitting poem for this time. The second step is to drain the accumulated water. The disaster relief branch has agreed with the general headquarters and the Junpu Bureau of the Yangtze River Conservancy Commission to borrow pumps from Shanghai for use in Hankou. The Yangtze River Conservancy Commission has appointed engineers Lin and Hu to assist in Hankou. It is expected to be ready within ten days and completely drained within two weeks. (September 7th)

He Jian Inspects Flood-stricken Counties 66

Changsha Correspondence: He Jian, accompanied by Zhou Yikui, a special commissioner sent by the central government to Hunan to inspect the flood disaster, Cao Bowen, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Chen Zongxiang, an engineer for disaster investigation, Lian Bishan, a technical expert from the Department of Civil Affairs, Cao Zonghai, a technical expert from the Department of Construction, Peng Maoyuan, the director of the Relief Committee, and others, went to the counties most severely affected by the disaster on the 31st of last month to inspect the flood disaster. It was originally intended to inspect Yuanjiang, Hanshou, Changde, Anxiang, Nanxian, Huarong, Fengxian, Yiyang, Xiangyin, Linxiang, Yueyang, and other counties, as well as the Jinggang area, before returning to the province. However, on the evening of the 3rd, an urgent telegram was received in Anxiang stating that the Guangdong-Guangxi armies had the appearance of invading Hunan, that the defense of southern Hunan was tight, and that He should return to the province early to preside over military affairs. He returned to the province by special ship from Anxiang on the 4th. All counties that had not been inspected were continued by Director Cao of the Department of Civil Affairs accompanied by Commissioner Zhou and others. It is reported that He and his party traveled by four small steamships from the province. On the evening of the 31st of last month, they arrived in Yuanjiang. They landed at 5:00 AM the next morning to inspect the disaster in the suburbs and finished at 8:00 AM. They returned to the ship at 10:00 AM and sailed to Hanshou, arriving at 4:00 PM. They immediately landed to inspect everything and finished at 6:00 PM. They attended a welcoming meeting at the county Party headquarters. They stayed in Hanshou that night. On the morning of the 2nd, they went to Changde at 6:00 AM. Due to the large waves along the way, they did not arrive in Changde until 2:00 PM. After landing, they inspected the flood disaster at the east and west gates. Then, they inspected the fortress project. On the morning of the 3rd, they sailed to Anxiang at 5:00 AM, arriving at 6:00 PM. They landed at the county Party headquarters and talked with representatives of various legal entities, and inquired about the suppression of bandits from Ma Kunshan, the deputy division commander of the 11th Division stationed in Anxiang. They returned to the ship at 9:00 PM. They originally planned to inspect Jinfeng the next day, but because they received a telegram from the province urging them to return, they returned to the province on the morning of the 4th at 5:00 AM, arriving at 10:00 PM that night. Among the inspections, the disaster in Yuanjiang was the most severe, with all the dikes and embankments in the county submerged, no harvest in the farmland, a loss of 5 to 6 million shi of grain, and tens of thousands of houses destroyed. The number of disaster victims is about 500,000 or more. Changde is the second most severely affected, followed by Anxiang and Hanshou. Currently, the water level on both sides has not fully receded. (September 6th)

The Southern and Northern Maoyou Dams in Jiangsu Have Been Opened 67

Water Level in the Lower Reaches of the Canal is Falling Daily

But Yi River Suddenly Reported to Be Discharging Again

Zhenjiang Correspondence: Yesterday, the provincial government received a telegram from the Dongtai Dafeng Company stating that the Southern and Central Maoyou dams had been opened, and the Northern Maoyou dam was being strongly urged to be opened by tenant farmers at the cost of their autumn harvest. They requested that troops not be deployed to suppress them and that funds be allocated quickly for work-relief programs. The original telegram is recorded below: (Chairman Ye of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, Telegraph Bureau, and transferred to Mr. Leng Yuqiu: Your telegrams of winter are respectfully acknowledged. The situation of the opening of the southern and central Maoyou dams has been respectfully reported in the winter. The northern Maoyou dam is also being strongly urged to be opened by tenant farmers who are willing to endure the pain and sacrifice the autumn harvest, and it was opened yesterday morning. There is no need for troops to suppress them. If troops have already been deployed, please request their withdrawal. At present, the water level is rising continuously. We are urging tenant farmers day and night to rush to repair the inner river in the hope of avoiding a common catastrophe. There are many disaster victims from outside the area who are being transported by the company's hired boats to within the area. They are crying for food and are in a pitiful state. The company's three dams are fully open, but the discharge of water is limited because the beaches are high and there are not many ports. Please allocate funds quickly to carry out work-relief programs and build more seaports to increase the flow, which will be of great benefit.)

Yangzhou Correspondence: In recent days, Yangzhou has seen an increasing number of disaster victims transported from various places, resulting in increased tension in the accommodation and relief work. However, in recent days, the water level in the lower reaches of the canal has been decreasing daily. According to the water gauge of the Shaobo Three-Ditch Sluice Gate, compared to before the breach of the dike, it has dropped by more than eleven feet. The magnitude of the water entering the lower river can already be seen. Furthermore, the flow of water in the canal has always been from north to south, but for the past ten days, regardless of whether it is high tide or not, it has been flowing from south to north, and the water is very clear, like the West Lake. The reason for this is unknown. However, it is heard that the Yi River is discharging again, which is causing considerable tension in the Huaiyin area. It is uncertain whether the great disaster will come to an end. It is not easy to completely block the breached areas for the time being. The administrative authorities believe that Jiangsu does not have the talent to block the breaches, and it is planned to recruit from the banks of the Yellow River to avoid unexpected events after the blocking. (September 7th)

Disaster Investigation Commissioners Arrive in Anhui One After Another 69

Provincial Relief Association Divides Flood Severity into Four Levels

More Than 9.48 Million Disaster Victims Throughout the Province

Anqing Correspondence: This year's flood in Anhui Province has been classified as the second most severe by the central government. Hong Hui, a disaster investigation commissioner of the Relief Committee, and Yan Zhuang, a relief commissioner of the Executive Yuan, have arrived in Anhui to investigate the disaster. Hong went to Dongliu, Qiupu, and other counties to investigate and returned to the province yesterday. He then took a small steamship to Guichi for investigation. Yan will go to Jiangxi in the coming days to discuss relief matters, leaving his attendant Sun Weidong in Anhui to handle matters. In addition, Tian Jiongjin, a commissioner of the Control Yuan, led his attendant Zhuo Hengzhi to Anhui on the Jiangxin ship at 6:00 AM on the 6th. He will go to the disaster areas for inspection in the coming days. The Anhui Provincial Relief Association was established on the 2nd of this month. The association, based on the approximate situation reported by the counties and with reference to the water situation of the Yangtze River, Huai River, lakes, and the composition of land and weirs, divided the counties with 60% to 80% damage into the first-class disaster area, 40% to 60% into the second-class disaster area, 30% to 40% into the third-class disaster area, and 20% to 30% into the fourth or fifth-class disaster area. There are a total of sixteen first-class disaster counties: Huaining, Tongcheng, Wangjiang, Wuwei, Hexian, Xuancheng, Guichi, Dongliu, Tongling, Wuhu, Fengyang, Shouxian, Fengtai, Huaiyuan, Huoqiu, and Wuhe. There are twelve second-class disaster counties: Susong, Hanshan, Dangtu, Fanchang, Suxian, Fuyang, Mengcheng, Guoyang, Yingshang, Sixian, Xuyi, and Tianchang. There are eight third-class disaster counties: Qianshan, Taihu, Hefei, Chaoxian, Lujiang, Qiupu, Lingbi, and Quanjiao. There are nine fourth-class disaster counties: Shucheng, Luan, Huoshan, Nanling, Dingyuan, Taihe, Haoxian, Chuxian, and Laian. There are three fifth-class disaster counties: Qingyang, Guangde, and Langxi. The total disaster area in the province is 1,803,400 li. The total number of disaster victims in the province is 9,485,000. The disaster area accounts for 37% of the total area of the province, and the disaster victims account for 44% of the total population of the province. After consulting with Yan and others, the distribution can be considered. (September 8th)

General Situation of the Disaster in Various Counties of Henan Province 70

▲ Sishui Recently, the Provincial Relief Association received a report from the relief branch in the county, stating that the land in Sishui is barren, and in years of good harvest, most of the food is supplied by neighboring counties. Once there is a poor harvest, they escape to beg for food. This year, there was a severe drought in the spring, and only 20% of the wheat was harvested. In the summer, there was continuous rain, and most of the autumn crops were not planted. Suddenly, in early August, torrential rain fell, which continued for many days. The autumn crops and houses on both sides of the Si River were submerged and collapsed, countless. The cities and towns nearby were engulfed by the whirlpool of the Yellow River, and the loss of material was countless. They were originally the survivors of soldiers and bandits, and nine out of ten families were empty. Now they have suffered such a terrible disaster. How can the people of Sishui survive? They can only weep and ask for relief to save the disaster victims. The Provincial Relief Association has reported the situation to the central government and appealed for relief.

▲ Yiyang The county Party Department telegraphed, stating that the land in Yiyang County is inherently poor. In recent years, locusts have bred, and there have been military disasters. The local vitality has been completely damaged. Moreover, bandit gangs are rampant, ravaging the entire territory. The people are in a situation where they have no way to escape. Since the summer, there have been continuous heavy rains, like pouring. The Dao Hai and Luo rivers collapsed at the same time. The houses in dozens of villages along the river, such as Lian Zhuang Li Qu, Sun Liu Hancheng, Liuquan, and Shuitan, became a bubble. Livestock was lost. Although the number of people who died in the water has not been clearly investigated, it is estimated that it is no less than hundreds. The Relief Association has sent commissioners to carry money to distribute emergency relief and has telegraphed all parties to appeal widely.

▲ Tanghe The county has fallen twice this year. The Cui and Wei bandits are inhuman. White bones are like mountains, filling the city and fields. The dead are gone, and the living are displaced. Everywhere is desolate. In June, July, and August, there was continuous rain. The Tang, Tong, and Bi rivers broke out at the same time, overflowing and flooding, accounting for 60% to 70% of the county. The depth of the water is about five feet above the ground. After the bandit atmosphere, there was a terrible disaster. The number of houses in the county that were destroyed and burned is countless. The Tang people have no hope. Although the Provincial Relief Association allocated 9,000 yuan for emergency relief, it is a drop in the bucket. Therefore, the county is now hoping that all parties will provide emergency relief quickly.

▲ Gongxian A flood occurred in the county, and all the houses in the city were submerged. The towns of Heishiguan, Sucun, and Xiaoyi were more than ten feet deep in water. According to the investigation report of the relief association, the general situation of the losses is as follows: (1) Number of affected villages: 120; (2) Affected square li: more than 630; (3) Submerged land: 160,000 mu; washed away land: 190,000 mu; (4) Number of affected households: more than 18,000 households, totaling 170,000 people; (5) Number of deaths: more than 90; (6) Number of livestock deaths: more than 120; (7) Number of houses collapsed: more than 50,000; (8) Loss of grain and property: more than 6 million yuan.

▲ Weishi Recently, the county relief branch reported to the Provincial Relief Association that the subordinate county is located on the south bank of the Yellow River. During the Qing Dynasty, the river breached its banks, and the entire territory became a sandbar. Wheat cannot be grown, and they rely on autumn crops for their livelihood. Last year, the county was沦入a war zone, with horizontal and vertical trenches. Because the people are unable to fill them, since summer, there has been continuous rain, lasting for days. The new and old Mai Lu rivers and the Shuangbi River successively collapsed, resulting in water depths of six to seven feet on the ground. The autumn crops were lost to the waves, and many houses became bubbles. The number of people and livestock who were drowned, crushed, and injured is uncountable. A vast expanse of water has become a marsh. The cries of desolation are heard throughout the fields. They are waiting for a way to provide relief. The Relief Association has sent telegrams to all parties to request relief and has sent commissioners to investigate.

The Third International and Soviet Russia's Conspiracy 71

Now, we will translate and record the publicly available content from the first section of the document:

(1) Outline of the Election Movement for Chinese Peasants, Workers, and Soldiers to Participate in the First National Soviet Congress (Excerpt from the Pamphlet "Outline of the Election Movement for Chinese Peasants, Workers, and Soldiers to Participate in the First National Soviet Congress")

The Central Preparatory Committee of the National Soviet Congress of Delegates of Peasants, Workers, and Soldiers has promulgated the regulations for electing delegates to the congress in Soviet and reactionary areas and has notified the preparatory committees and public organizations to intensify the election movement according to these instructions. The National Congress has been postponed to February 7, 1931. However, given the improper preparations by the preparatory committees in various regions, the Central Preparatory Committee has had to urge these committees and public organizations to intensify the election movement and to announce the following election outline so that the election movement in various regions can be consistent with the instructions of the Central Committee and the National Congress can be successful. (1) The Significance of the First National Soviet Congress of Delegates and its Election Movement: The convening of the First National Congress of Delegates of Chinese Peasants, Workers, and Soldiers is occurring when the Chinese Soviet revolutionary movement, under the leadership of the proletariat, is fiercely attacking the reactionary politics of the imperialist Kuomintang, and also when the imperialist powers and the Kuomintang warlords

Page 11

Important News

are jointly attacking the Soviet regime. The purpose of the Congress is to unify and consolidate the power of the Soviets throughout the country and to establish the highest power of the peasants, workers, and soldiers under the dictatorship of the Soviet central government. Therefore, all preparatory committees and revolutionary organizations should closely organize the mass election movement. (2) The Nature and Tasks of the Election Movement: The National Soviet Congress election movement held in the current period of class struggle aims to carry out class organization and establish the power of the working masses. (3) The Class Perspective of the Election Movement: The election movement should be carried out among the working masses, and the leadership of the proletariat should be fully guaranteed in this movement. Landlord oppressors, factory and shop owners who exploit with usury, rich peasants, and all reactionary elements should be deprived of their right to vote so that they cannot participate in Soviet organs and undermine the dictatorship of the peasants and workers. (4) On the Propaganda Work of the Election Movement: Propaganda work should be carried out by systematic and responsible individuals. Propaganda work includes the distribution of propaganda materials, the organization of speaking teams, the establishment of reading groups and civilian schools, and the establishment of communication organs. Red labor unions should find ways to conduct propaganda among factory workers and shop employees, organize a propaganda department in each factory or shop, and inform them of the political power and good living conditions enjoyed by workers in the Soviet areas. Rural red organizations should incite peasants to refuse to pay taxes and rents and refuse to repay debts. Intensive propaganda should be carried out among soldiers to make them understand the good treatment received by soldiers in the Soviet areas and encourage them to desert their posts and join the Red Army with their weapons. (5) The Election Movement and Mass Struggle: The purpose of the election movement should be to transform the economic struggles of the masses into political struggles, paying particular attention to sailors, soldiers, factory workers, and railway workers. (6) Mass Organizations in the Election Movement: 1. Absorb the masses into red organizations; 2. Develop and expand the organization of red peasants in non-Soviet areas; 3. Organize soldiers' committees in the army; 4. Consolidate the organizations of the poor peasant associations, revolutionary mutual aid societies, anti-imperialist leagues, and revolutionary student federations. (7) The Method of Election: Each organization should hold separate meetings to elect representatives to participate in the election movement. Electors should be warned to carefully elect qualified individuals as representatives. (8) Preparation for the General Election Congress: A preparatory committee should be organized to handle the preparations for the general election congress. When the general election congress is held, security guards and children's corps should be dispatched to maintain order. (5) The Work of Delegates Participating in the First Election: The delegate should undertake the following tasks: 1. Engage in activities in factories, rural areas, and barracks; 2. Recruit members for red labor unions; 3. Promote the National Soviet Congress of Delegates; 4. Raise funds for the election movement. (10) The Work of the National Congress after the Final Election: After the final election is completed, the National Congress should convene newly elected delegates to familiarize them with the details of Soviet duties. The above outline must be strictly observed and implemented by all election movement preparatory committees.

(8) Report from the Eastern Hubei Special Committee on the Defeat of the Red Army

The number of enemy troops in Yangxin is four regiments, in Daye two regiments, in Tongshan one regiment, and in Wuning two regiments. Thus, our situation is becoming increasingly difficult. The enemy troops in Yangxin are now actively attacking us, and we can only defend three strategic points, the rest have been seized by the enemy. They have also organized local militias everywhere, which are also a considerable force. People from various places have been fleeing back to our side one after another in recent days, making it particularly difficult to provide supplies. Other areas, such as Daye and Wuning, are also seeing daily reductions, which is extremely serious. The advance of our Red Army's Third Army is too slow. All the firearms are only enough for nine hundred men. Previously, we sent a battalion to Xiushui to contact the 16th Army, so the current number is only two battalions. Coupled with the lack of bullets and the ineffectiveness of lower-level cadres, we have suffered more than one setback. Our work in the white areas has also been fruitless. However, at this critical moment, we are unwilling to sit and wait for death, so we have decided to send a portion of our forces and the people to fight the enemy, while the remaining forces will be used for rear-area defense. When the battalion sent to Xiushui is recalled, we will unite the armed masses and fight the enemy to the death. The enemy troops have now retreated into the city and dare not station in the countryside, fearing losses. Although we do not have sophisticated equipment, our combat performance in the white areas is considerable. It is a pity that our organizational work cannot keep pace with the military, so we are actively developing party work in the white areas, organizing the masses, and creating economic and political struggles to match the military. In the red areas, we will pay more attention to equipping the people with weapons and finding ways to expand our propaganda among the enemy troops. (The enemy soldiers who are subjected to our propaganda mostly fire into the air and do not aim at the people; however, the organization of the army is not yet perfect, so there have been no large-scale defections so far.) The general public has a good attitude towards us. The people of the areas that were once Soviet areas but have been seized by the enemy can all recall the benefits of the Soviet government. Therefore, our work in the white areas is still easy to do, but they have not received news from various places north of the Yangtze River for a long time. Although the organizations in these places still exist, the Soviet government has been completely eliminated. Eastern Hubei Special Committee, May 12. (To be continued)

Shandong Provincial Government to Purchase Books from the Haiyuan Pavilion 72

Agreed on a Half-Donation, Half-Sale Arrangement

Jinan Correspondence: The Shandong Provincial Library is in contact with the Yang family of Haiyuan Pavilion in Liaocheng, Shandong, to arrange a half-donation, half-sale arrangement to allow the Shandong Provincial Government to preserve the collection. This matter has been brewing for many years, with ups and downs and much effort. Preliminary agreement was reached last month, but the Shibu incident occurred, and military affairs became urgent, so the matter was shelved again. Now that the situation has stabilized, the old case has been brought up again, and the two sides have largely reached an agreement. According to Wang Fangting, Director of the Department of Industry, Chairman Han has recently agreed to the case of purchasing the books from Haiyuan Pavilion for preservation by the provincial government. After some further procedures, a decision can be made. He suggests that the funds for purchasing the books could be advanced by the provincial government first. After the books are transported, a contract could be signed with the Commercial Press to print and sell them, and pre-sale vouchers could be issued. The books are all well-known and rare, and would not be difficult to sell. The book funds of three to five hundred thousand yuan could then be returned to the provincial treasury. In this way, the Yang family would receive the funds, Shandong would preserve the ancient books, and they would be widely circulated throughout the country, achieving several benefits in one stroke. Wang Xiantang, the director of the library, is currently visiting libraries in various places, and a plan can be studied when he returns to Jinan. According to reports, the Nanjing Library initially argued that the books from Haiyuan Pavilion should be kept in the central location, while the Peiping Library argued that they should be kept in the old capital, the cultural center. Each side held its own reasons, leading to a long period of unresolved issues. Finally, it was decided that they would be kept in Shandong, but the issue of the book price repeatedly caused complications. During this period, Lao Zhichang, the former Minister of Communications, because of his relationship with the book owner Yang Jingfu as father-in-law and son-in-law, made considerable efforts. Finally, a half-donation, half-sale arrangement was agreed upon, with the Song Dynasty editions of the Four Books and Five Classics remaining with the Yang family, and the remaining books being transferred. In the future, well-known figures and appraisers will be invited to publicly evaluate them, and the Shandong Provincial Government will pay half the value (approximately 300,000 yuan). A Haiyuan Pavilion will be built in the library to preserve the books and commemorate Yang's contribution in donating the books. All parties have agreed on this matter, and there should be no other changes. A decision on the implementation plan can be made when Han Fuju and Wang Xiantang return to Jinan.

Results of Investigation into the Fujian Paper Bamboo Shoot Tax Case 73

Lin Dingxun and Zheng Jinqing Transferred to the Court for Investigation

Zhang Zhedan Received a Major Demerit for Ineffective Handling of Affairs

The Provincial Party Headquarters Still Requests the Central Government to Investigate He Gonggan

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Fujian Department of Finance discovered the details of the paper bamboo shoot business tax fraud case, which has been reported previously. It is now learned that the Department of Education Director Cheng Shigui and the Department of Finance Director He Gonggan, who were dispatched by the provincial government to investigate the case, found six major suspicious points: (1) Lin Dingxun, the director of the Paper Bamboo Shoot Business Tax Bureau, previously admitted to the Department of Finance that he had partners, but now he is reversing himself, contradicting himself. If there were no illegal shareholders involved, why would he try so hard to conceal it? (2) Lin Dingxun started collecting taxes in June, but the contract document stated that it started on July 1st, and he concealed the tax revenue for June and did not report it, which is suspected of embezzlement of public funds. (3) A search of Lin Dingxun's residence found more than 200 letters from before 1919, but none of the letters from this year were found, which is suspected of destroying evidence. (4) The account books for the paper bamboo shoot tax declaration and the account books of the Paper Bamboo Shoot Tax Bureau have already been submitted to the Department of Finance for review, but the tax receipts that should be submitted for inspection were repeatedly urged before they were submitted, and the ink on the seam was smudged, which is suspected of tampering. (5) Zheng Jinqing, the specialist for paper bamboo shoot tax, has been handling tax affairs for many years and is very familiar with the situation. However, he arbitrarily lowered the tax amount that has always been collected for more than 200,000 yuan, entrusting Lin Dingxun to handle it for 150,000 yuan, and even after repeated reports, he still sided with him. At first, he wrongly judged that the amount could not be increased, and then he did not only not criticize but also deemed appropriate and forwarded to the record Lin Dingxun's report of the peak season as off-season and the concealment of the June tax revenue, which shows that he colluded with Lin Dingxun to embezzle tax revenue, which is a major suspicion. (6) Zhang Zhedan, the acting director of the Business Tax Bureau, has experience in consumption tax affairs. However, after the clerk Su Wenbing revealed the corruption, he did not conduct a detailed audit or make a clear statement, which is not free from the appearance of skillfully avoiding responsibility. The details of the investigation have now been reported to the provincial government for decision. The provincial government committee decided the previous day that Lin Dingxun and Zheng Jinqing are indeed suspected of major corruption and should be transferred to the court for investigation and handling according to law. Zhang Zhedan should receive a major demerit for ineffective handling of affairs. Su Wenbing is diligent and commendable and should be promoted to show reward and encouragement. The business tax should be seriously reorganized by the Department of Finance, and the situation should be reported in detail for review and handling. However, the Provincial Party Headquarters believes that He Gonggan, the director of the Department of Finance, is suspected of communicating with Zhang Zhedan, Zheng Jinqing, and Lin Dingxun to jointly commit corruption, embezzle large sums of money, and destroy evidence. At the previous standing committee meeting, it was argued that since He Gonggan is the main person in this case, it is inappropriate for the provincial government to appoint him as the special investigator. It was decided to send a telegram to the central government and request the National Government to first suspend He Gonggan from his post and then send a special investigator to Fujian to investigate the case. Yesterday, another telegram was sent to the central government, requesting that He be dismissed from his post and investigated. (September 4)

Wuhu Express 74

▲After the major flood in Wuhu, it was followed by a strong wind, and thousands of disaster victims were swept into the water by huge waves and drowned. Clean corpses are floating everywhere, and the various charitable organizations are unable to recover them all. The Provincial Department of Civil Affairs specifically telegraphed the county government to quickly find ways to hire boats for recovery and burial to prevent epidemics.

▲Since Anhui rice was banned from being transported out of the province, although the prevention and control efforts in various counties have been strict, there are still many who smuggle it out of the country. There are more paddy fields in the Sanhe and Shucheng areas under the jurisdiction of Hefei in central Anhui, and it is estimated that more than 100,000 shi of surplus rice can be transported out. A few days ago, a rice merchant surnamed Wang from Hefei purchased several thousand shi of rice in the Sanhe area, using fourteen large civilian boats towed by two small steamers. However, when they reached Yuxikou, they were discovered and detained by the joint defense and self-defense corps of the three counties of He, Hanshan, and Wuwei. Wang and others have now come to Wuhu to find ways to resolve the issue.

▲The Anhui Provincial Government convened a provincial-level disaster relief conference to discuss the relief and reconstruction plans for the disaster areas throughout the province. Zhai Zhancheng, the representative of the Wuhu Flood Relief Association, and Wu Xingzhou, the representative of the Chamber of Commerce, were summoned to the province yesterday to attend the meeting.

▲According to the audit of the Wuhu Flood Relief Association, the current emergency relief and future spring relief will require no less than 1.5 million yuan. Ways to raise funds are currently being coordinated, but there is a concern that the recent emergency relief will not be able to meet the immediate needs. A telegram was sent to the provincial government again today, requesting approval to designate Wuhu as a special disaster area and to allocate a large sum of money first for relief.

▲Yesterday, the Wuhu County Government captured five bandits, including Wang Yongzhen, who were intercepting travelers in Yitaiwei. They were executed by shooting at the railway embankment today. (6th)

Local Correspondence

Suzhou 75

Continuous Kidnappings Occur in Guangfu Township. Bandit Activity is Rampant in Various Townships Along Taihu Lake. Kidnapping cases are heard of every day. The authorities have no way to suppress them. On the night of the 7th, at about 10:00 p.m., more than 20 bandits suddenly came to No. 2 Chongshan Temple Front Street, Guangfu Township, Taihu Lake, and kidnapped the homeowner, Gu Kaishe, and his son, Yaoming. Then, they went to Dongbang and kidnapped a person named Sun Honggao, heading towards South Taihu Lake.

The Department of Finance Corrects Official Land Mistaken as Public Property. Wu Kunjian from the Official Property Bureau submitted a report to the Department of Finance stating that the ownerless official land in Wu County had been mistakenly classified as public property and requesting correction. Subsequently, the Department of Finance instructed that since there is a register of public property in Wu County, it should naturally be used as the basis. If it is not listed in the register, how can the transfer by the Finance Bureau be used as a basis for public ownership, thereby encroaching on official land? The Wu County Government should be instructed to quickly make corrections based on the register to emphasize the importance of official property. The bureau then forwarded a letter to the county government, scheduling a meeting of relevant agencies to follow the department's instructions and implement the division based on the original register to clarify the boundaries.

Water Police Detectives Capture Notorious Robbers. Xiong Bin, a patrol officer from the 2nd District Department of the Provincial Public Security Force stationed in Wuxi Water, along with Detective Zhou and others, captured three robbers, Tang Jinbao, Wang Maolang, and Chen Baolang, a few days ago in Yangming Road. They were interrogated in the district and confessed to several accomplices. Yesterday, Detective Zhou Rugang, along with detective Chen Xiang and others, went to Zhaotian, a remote mountain area in Hudai, and captured three more bandits, Wang Shenglin, his younger brother Wang Xigen, and a helper, Chen Tingyuan. They were immediately interrogated and confessed to the robbery cases in Qingshanwan and Shuiding Lane. They are being detained pending review. The robber Wang Shenglin is strong and proficient in martial arts. He was a member of the guard team under Mao Xueqin, a Red bandit in Jiangyin. He is also responsible for the cases of shooting and killing Chen Guankui and Luo Shixiong in Shanzhen Bridge, as well as using the party to intimidate and defraud the families of Wang Zengfu and Zhou Guozhen in Xiwujie Bridge. Ten Thousand Mu of Dike Refugees Temporarily Stay in Zhangzhu. According to news from the navigation sector yesterday, this year in Yixing, there has been continuous rain and rising floodwaters, submerging low-lying fields. Ten thousand mu of dikes and nearby farmlands have been completely submerged. There will be no harvest this autumn, and the grass huts where the villagers live have been washed away, leaving them with nowhere to live. Therefore, they have had to leave their homes, supporting the old and carrying the young, seeking refuge in the Chenghuang Temple in Zhangzhu Town, with a total of more than 200 men and women. They are covered in dirt and are quite pitiful. Merchants in the town are providing food, which is proving difficult to sustain.

The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, from Hangzhou to Ningbo, had its Caoe River railway bridge construction delayed due to the sudden outbreak of the European War sixteen years ago, which led to the German engineers returning to their country, causing inconvenience to passengers. The Ministry of Railways, noting the high number of passengers and busy transportation in Ningbo, Shaoxing, and Hangzhou, plans to use the Italian Boxer Indemnity to complete the route. The Shaoxing-Caoe section will be built first to facilitate transportation. Shangyu 87

Losses from the Floods in the Southwest. Since the hurricane and torrential rain on the nights of the 24th and 25th of last month, countless lives have been lost and property losses have exceeded one million. The following is a record of the news received daily from various sources: (1) Outside the Yuansha Mound embankment, about five miles from Baiguan, was breached by the tidal bore. Seventeen households of residents, except for three who escaped, were all buried in the bellies of fish. (2) Along the coast of Lihai, the residents' huts and firewood sheds were washed away by the water. The cotton in the sandy land was almost entirely broken by the wind. (3) At the Yuya Eight-Community Embankment, more than five miles from Zhangzhen, the Shun River's seventy-two tributary streams surged due to the flood from Sheng, causing five breaches, with the Chi Lake Dam being the most severe, stretching over four hundred feet. The water was over ten feet high on the flat ground, and over five hundred thousand acres of crops within the affected area were completely destroyed. The Wantou and Nanpu embankments, about five miles from the town, though not collapsed, suffered significant damage with fields and crops submerged. The Oupu Embankment, about ten miles from the town, is an important defense line for Wantou, Nanpu, and other hillside areas. The embankment site is over ten feet wide and over two feet high, and the construction was not weak. However, the land is entirely sandy, and the mountain torrents from the Du Zhai Ridge suddenly erupted, catching the residents off guard and causing a collapse with a breach of over one hundred feet. The deaths of people and livestock and the submersion of fields and crops are countless. It is estimated that over eighty villages and settlements throughout the town are affected, with the disaster area accounting for eight tenths of the total.

Educational News

Special Report

Opinions on Compiling University Curriculum 88

Chen Zhongfan

The compilation of university curriculum should have a certain objective and a consistent plan, so as to avoid being fragmented and lacking a system. Looking at the recent universities' implementation of the elective course system, apart from stipulating that Chinese, English, and Mathematics are compulsory courses for the first year, the rest are up to the students to choose by department. Thus, they choose what interests them most, seeking only specialization, regardless of order. Overreaching and aiming too high is the nature of youth, and there is nothing strange about it. However, the negative consequences are that students often lack general knowledge and have a weak foundation. Even if they proceed to study specialized topics and expert theories, they only scratch the surface and gain nothing of substance. For schools, opening too many courses cannot be handled by three or five full-time teachers, requiring the hiring of many part-time lecturers, wasting funds. For teachers, the scope of courses they teach is too narrow, and the teaching materials are scarce, forcing them to patch things up and muddle through. To correct these ills, I propose to reorganize the university curriculum as follows:

(1) Curriculum

University curriculum is divided into four categories: 1. Compulsory Public Courses, 2. Elective Public Courses, 3. Compulsory Major Courses, 4. Elective Minor Courses. The first two years are for completing categories one and two, and the last two years are for studying categories three and four.

(1) Compulsory Public Courses

1. Party Ideology: This course lectures on the Three Principles of the People, the Fundamentals of National Reconstruction, the Outline of National Reconstruction, and Dr. Sun Yat-sen's theories. Two hours of instruction per week, completed in one year, for a total of four credits.

2. Basic Chinese: This course focuses on prose, supplemented by poetry and lyrics, emphasizing practice, and requiring extracurricular reading of famous authors' collections. Three hours of instruction and one hour of practice per week, completed in one year, for a total of six credits.

3. Basic English: This course, in addition to lecturing, emphasizes practice, extracurricular reading of books and newspapers, and holding speeches and debates. Three hours of instruction and one hour of practice per week, completed in one year, for a total of six credits.

4. Second Foreign Language: Choose one of French, German, or Japanese. Students of literature may choose to study Latin. Three hours per week, completed in one year, for a total of six credits.

5. Military Training: According to the plans of the Directorate General of Military Training, completed in two years, for a total of six credits.

6. Physical Education and Hygiene: Universities should set up several specialists in physical education and hygiene guidance, who will lecture on physical education and hygiene theories, supervise and encourage students to participate in various sports, form hygienic habits, and correct bad habits. Completed in four years, without credit.

The above compulsory public courses total twenty-eight credits.

(2) Elective Public Courses, divided into five groups:

First Group

1. Methodology of Science: 3 credits

2. History of Scientific Development: 3 credits

3. Physics: 6 credits

4. Chemistry: 6 credits

5. Biology: 6 credits

The purpose of this group of courses is to enable students to use scientific methods, understand the general situation and laws of the natural world, and train their clear minds and meticulous thinking. Select twelve credits.

Second Group

1. Modern Chinese History (Last Hundred Years): 3 credits

2. History of Western Culture: 3 credits

3. Overview of Modern Civilization: 3 credits

4. Current Status of International Politics and Economics: 3 credits

5. Current Status of Chinese Politics and Economics: 3 credits

6. Social Structure and Its Evolution: 3 credits

The purpose of this group of courses is to enable students to understand the era in which they live and the cultural status of their society and country, and their interrelationships. Select twelve credits.

Third Group

1. History of Chinese Philosophy: 6 credits

2. History of Western Philosophy: 6 credits

3. Philosophy of Life: 3 credits

4. Logic: 3 credits

The purpose of these courses is to enable students to synthesize knowledge from various subjects and further seek the overall universal principles and the meaning of life. Select twelve credits.

Fourth Group

1. Chinese Literature: 6 credits

2. Western Literature: 6 credits

3. Introduction to Art: 3 credits

4. History of Western Art: 3 credits

The purpose of this group of courses is to enable students to understand literary trends and their interests, thereby cultivating noble personalities. Select twelve credits.

Fifth Group

1. Applied Chemistry: 6 credits

2. Handicrafts: 6 credits

3. Horticulture: 6 credits

4. Animal Husbandry: 6 credits

The purpose of this group of courses is to enable students to acquire a specialized skill that can be applied in practice. Female students may substitute with domestic science, cooking, and sewing. Select six credits.

The above five groups, totaling fifty-four credits, are completed in the first and second years.

3. Compulsory Major Courses: Approximately 30 to 50 credits

4. Elective Minor Courses: Approximately 20 credits

(2) Credit Allocation

First and Second Semesters: Approximately 20 to 22 credits, totaling 40-44

Third and Fourth Semesters: Same as above, 40-44

Fifth and Sixth Semesters: Approximately 15 to 20 credits, 30-40

Seventh and Eighth Semesters: Approximately 10 to 15 credits, 20-30

Total: Approximately 130 to 150 credits, 130-150

(3) Examinations

After completing the compulsory and elective public courses in the first and second years, in addition to the temporary examinations by the teachers in charge, the examination committee will conduct a selective joint examination. Those who pass will be given a diploma for the preliminary stage of university and will be allowed to enter the various colleges to receive departmental education and study the major and minor programs.

(4) Expenses

As mentioned above, in the first and second years, only the Colleges of Arts and Sciences need to open public compulsory and elective courses for students to choose from. Other colleges do not need to open separate courses, and the expenses for the first and second years can be entirely transferred for equipment and research. Compared with the current system, the expenses will definitely be reduced.

(5) Equipment

Currently, universities, except for natural sciences which are supplemented by experiments, rarely emphasize practical surveys and tests in other social sciences. As for literature, art, philosophy, and other subjects, there are no opportunities for discussion and exercises other than classroom lectures. In the future, research rooms for various subjects should be added, displaying various reference materials for students to browse independently, and specifying discussion times for teachers and students to exchange ideas.

(6) Advisors

Currently, some university teachers hold courses at two or three schools concurrently, rushing around all day, with students having very little opportunity to interact, let alone learn from each other. In the future, we should find ways to increase salaries, restrict concurrent classes, and have full-time teachers serve as advisors, guiding students in the research room at specified times each week for practical research.

The above is a rough statement of my personal opinions, hoping that people in the country will provide corrections.

Important News

Measures for the Education Sector to Donate Funds for Disaster Relief 89

The Ministry of Education has issued a notice to the universities and educational institutions directly under its jurisdiction and the education departments of various provinces and cities regarding the measures for teachers and staff of public schools and employees of educational institutions to donate funds for disaster relief. The notice refers to the administrative order No. 4323 of the Executive Yuan (referring to the instruction No. 439 of the National Government), which approved the letter from the Central Political Council (approved the letter from the Central Executive Committee), stating that "In view of the great flood disasters in various places, the Standing Committee has discussed and decided that all national officials and employees of state-owned enterprises, teachers and staff of public schools, employees of public educational institutions, and comrades working in party headquarters, whose monthly salary is above 100 yuan, should donate 5%; those above 200 yuan should donate 10%; those above 400 yuan should donate 15%; and those above 600 yuan should donate 20%, for a period of three months. However, since this measure covers all political and military agencies across the country, it should be decided by the Political Council and implemented by the government." The letter is specially recorded and communicated to you, hoping that you will investigate and handle accordingly and reply. The matter was submitted to the 286th meeting of the conference for discussion and a decision was made to handle it. The various agencies should give priority to deducting the flood relief donations in September, October and November of this year. Apart from the donation of comrades working in party headquarters, which has been communicated to the Central Executive Committee for handling, the corresponding case is recorded and communicated to you, hoping that you will investigate and handle accordingly and reply. Based on this approval, the decision was made at the tenth regular meeting of the government to handle the case and issue a general order for compliance. In addition to issuing a reply and separate orders, the order urgently requires you to comply with the above handling and inform your subordinates to comply with the order. In addition to issuing separate orders, this order is combined to order the relevant department to comply with the order. This order is hereby given.

Zhejiang Province's Educational Administrative Guidelines and Implementation Plan 90

As the year 20 is approaching, the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education has formulated the Zhejiang Province's Educational Administrative Guidelines and the Implementation Plan for the year 20 as the basis for progress, which are recorded separately below:

A. Administrative Guidelines 91

(1) Promote the function of the Three Principles of the People on education and culture, so that the education of the province is completely based on the Three Principles of the People. (2) In addition to examination, correction or sanctions for various educational matters, special attention is paid to political and educational institutions, instilling the spirit of academicization and enhancing the general interest in academic research. (4) In the training of national morality, emphasis is placed on maintaining the inherent morality of the Chinese nation and cultivating the habits of diligence and thrift, and the spirit of sacrifice and struggle. (5) In planning, emphasis is placed on the attitude of research, the method of experimentation, and the basis of factual statistics. (6) In the facilities of educational institutions and the assessment of educational funds, special attention is paid to the principles of economy and efficiency. (7) Education is recognized as a single and permanent undertaking, on the one hand, to improve the material and spiritual environment of the education sector as much as possible, and on the other hand, to reward the contributions of educational talents to education. (8) Seek the equal development of education in provinces, cities and counties, and at all levels, so that school education and social education can progress simultaneously. (9) Abide by the educational goals promulgated by the Central Government, with special emphasis on health education, science education and civic education. (10) Pay attention to the universalization and popularization of educational effectiveness and realize equal opportunities in education.

B. Implementation Plan 92

(1) Regarding general matters

1. Examine the facilities of various educational institutions and supervise the implementation of the educational purposes and implementation guidelines passed by the Third National Congress. 2. Link up or entrust academic institutions, groups or experts to study various educational problems in the province. 3. Review the supervisory guidance outline of each county and city. 4. Continue to supervise the progress of school district and county and city guidance conferences. 5. Hold the Second Provincial Guidance Conference. 6. Introduce the educational advantages of each county and city. 7. Hold the Second Provincial Education Achievement Exhibition. 8. Plan to set up an educational supplies reference hall. 9. Continue to collect various educational publications. 10. Formulate and implement health education measures. 11. Formulate educational institution construction regulations. 12. Formulate a plan to promote phonetic symbols and supervise its implementation. 13. Send personnel to investigate various educational issues at home and abroad.

(2) Regarding Party Ideology Education Matters

1. Supervise educational institutions to earnestly study Party Ideology and the implementation of Party Ideology Education. 2. Supervise various educational institutions to complete the necessary equipment for the implementation of Party Ideology Education. 3. Inspect and assess the performance of Party Ideology Education in various educational institutions. 4. Continue to assess the performance of teachers and staff at all levels in studying Party Ideology. 5. Ban all publications that violate Party Ideology and Party Program. 6. Formulate methods for linking various course assignments with Party Ideology. 7. Encourage and promote excellent works of music, art, literature, etc. that promote Party Ideology.

(3) Regarding Educational Funding Matters

1. Actively plan and gradually implement ways to open up sources of local educational funding. 2. Revise the management methods for district educational funding and township educational funding. 3. Supervise various counties and cities to sort out educational property and school fields. 4. Formulate measures for various counties and cities to distribute funds to educational institutions. 5. Formulate measures for provincial funds to subsidize educational funding in various counties. 6. Promulgate measures to subsidize the funding of teacher training institutions in various counties and cities. 7. Revise the interim regulations on subsidizing the funding of county-established, co-established, and private secondary schools and above. 8. Formulate a property list for provincial educational institutions. 9. Clean up the backlog of transfers of affiliated institutions. 10. Raise funds to repay the outstanding expenses of affiliated institutions. 11. Supervise various counties and cities to handle the registration of private primary school property. 12. Formulate measures for compensating for the abuse of educational funds.

(4) Regarding Higher Education Matters

1. Plan to add various specialized schools. 2. Continue to investigate graduates from Zhejiang Province who have attended specialized schools and above at home and abroad, and conduct registration. 3. Investigate the service status of graduates from Zhejiang Province who have attended specialized schools and above in the country.

Municipal Education Bureau Orders Extension of the Registration Period for Primary and Secondary Schools 95

Extended to the end of the year 20

The Municipal Education Bureau announced yesterday: "Previously, the Ministry of Education ordered that the deadline for the registration of private schools was approaching. Those who failed to apply for registration after the deadline could be dealt with separately in accordance with the previous order. However, considering that various schools may have special difficulties, the registration deadline is extended as appropriate. The deadline for schools above the specialized school level is extended to the end of June of the year 21. The departments of education in the respective provinces and cities shall determine the extended period for schools below the secondary school level. Those who still fail to apply for registration after the deadline will be ordered to stop recruiting students or be ordered to close down. Now, this bureau has approved the extension of the registration deadline for secondary schools and below in this city to the end of the year 20. Those who still fail to apply for registration after the deadline will be stopped from recruiting students or ordered to close down in accordance with the Ministry of Education's order. The relevant orders have been presented to the Ministry of Education for approval and are now being announced. All schools that need to be registered should quickly follow the rules to apply for registration, and do not wait and see and delay yourselves."

First Disaster Relief Basketball Game: Chih Chih Unluckily Suffers Defeat 96

Result: 24 to 28, Hsi Ching Wins

See you again tomorrow night at 7:30 PM

Chih Chih, which is famous in the south of the Yangtze River, and Hsi Ching team, which is highly regarded in Shanghai, played a disaster relief basketball game at the Chinese Basketball Hall last night at 7:30 PM. People from all walks of life enthusiastically participated, numbering nearly a thousand, with excellent results. Chih Chih had a strong momentum throughout the game, consistently taking the lead. Unexpectedly, in the last three minutes, they suddenly showed a scattered phenomenon, resulting in a four-point difference and falling behind. The result was 24 to 28. The two teams will meet again tomorrow night at 7:30 PM, and there will be another bloody battle to determine the outcome.

Donations Near 500 97

Those who appreciate basketball skills are certainly unwilling to miss this good opportunity, and the income is entirely for disaster relief purposes. Considering both public and private interests, spending six jiao is a good deal. There were 644 tickets sold, and the tickets sold by Chih Chih and Hsi Ching have not yet been received. The total is estimated to be about a thousand, with donations near 500 yuan.

The Focus of Victory or Defeat 98

Victory or defeat is commonplace for soldiers, and there is no need to dwell on it, but it is necessary to seek the focus of victory or defeat in order to improve strategies and achieve all-round talent. The athletes of Chih Chih are undoubtedly agile and skilled in basketball. However, their inaccurate long shots, excessive fouls, and too few follow-up shots unfortunately led to their defeat to Hsi Ching. The formation of Hsi Ching is not as neat as that of Chih Chih, but it is more stable. Their victory lies in fewer fouls and more free throws. Hsi Ching scored eight points from free throws and committed four fouls, while Chih Chih scored two points from free throws and committed eleven fouls. Hsi Ching scored six more points. In terms of the number of goals scored, Chih Chih scored eleven goals (22 points) and Hsi Ching scored ten goals (20 points). Chih Chih scored one more goal. In comparison, Chih Chih had the ability to win.

The Tension of Combat 99

The tense combat between the two sides was exhilarating. Pi Sheng scored a free throw, breaking the silence in the basketball hall. Gu Guangdao and Kong Guangyi followed suit, putting Chih Chih in the lead. Shi Kuiya and Shi Misi worked hard, creating a 4-4 tie. Chih Chih first, Hsi Ching later. After 4-4, there were continuous 6-6 and 8-8 ties. Qian Dingshen relied on his clever figure to play with the giant Nepolo as if he were in the palm of his hand. At halftime, Chih Chih led 15 to 14, gaining one more point. In the second half, Shi Kuiya was transferred to the forward position, and Ta Fula replaced him. In the situation between the two sides, Chih Chih still maintained the leading position. Yang Lin Yu and Qian Dingshen attacked the enemy's fortresses once, with a score of 22 to 18. Hsi Ching stepped up their work, and soon it became a 22 tie. At that time, there were three minutes of silence, with no records. Chih Chih's vigor suddenly fell, losing three consecutive goals. At the end, Qian Dingshen scored only one goal, resulting in a 24 to 28 defeat.

Finance Group to Announce Collection of Donations

Zhu Qinglan Expresses Opinions on Guiding the Huai River

Japanese Circles to Donate 400,000 in Relief Funds

Song Ziwen, Chairman of the National Government Relief Committee for Flood Disasters, convened the second standing committee meeting of various committee members at 5:30 PM the night before last. Last night at 5:00 PM, he convened the committee members again for discussions. It was decided to hold a general meeting of all committee members at the Central Bank at 3:00 PM this afternoon to discuss plans for relieving flood disasters in various regions and allocating donations. At the same time, the committee's finance group and disaster area work group announced the second batch of donations received by the group yesterday, along with Mr. Zhu Qinglan's opinions on guiding the Huai River. Details are recorded as follows:

▲Finance Group Continues to Receive Donations The finance group of the committee announced yesterday the amount of the second batch of donations received as follows: 300,000 yuan from Chinese and foreign personnel of the national customs, 80,000 yuan from all members of the Money Trade Association, 60,000 yuan each from the Beijing, Tianjin, and Philippines branches of the National Government Relief Committee for Flood Disasters, 30,000 yuan from the Batavia branch, 20,000 yuan from the Chahar branch, 50,000 yuan from the owner of Jardine Matheson & Co., 10,000 yuan each from the Four Banks Savings Society, Jin Cheng Bank, Continental Bank, Y盐业 Bank, Zhongnan Bank, and China Industrial Bank, 10,006 yuan from the Philippine Chinese Rice Merchants Association, 7,500 yuan each from British American Tobacco Company, 5,000 yuan from Zhongxing, 4,000 yuan from Jiangsu Bank, 3,000 yuan from Tung Hwa Trust Company, 10,000 yuan from Mr. Zheng Bozhao, 5,000 yuan from Mr. Wu Qifan, 6,000 yuan from the Yingkou Shipping Association, 5,000 yuan from Asiatic Petroleum Company, and 3,000 yuan from Da Lai Shipping Company, totaling 791,006 yuan.

▲Zhu Qinglan Suggests Guiding the Huai River into the Sea To Fundamentally Solve Flood Disasters in the Huai River Basin and Implement Relief Efforts, Guiding the Huai River Should Be Undertaken as a Matter of Utmost Urgency. Upon Reviewing the Plan Announced by the Huai River Guidance Committee, Although It Was Carefully Designed in Advance and Approved by the National Government, the Unprecedented Simultaneous Rise of the Yangtze and Huai Rivers Has Created a New Record. The Unknown Further Rise of the Huai River in the Fifth Year of the Republic of China, as Proposed by the 万国红十字会 民三, Has Likewise Lost Its Basis. Based on My Limited Understanding, I Briefly Offer the Following: (A) Guiding the Huai River into the Sea. Discussions on Whether to Guide the Huai River into the Yangtze or into the Sea Have Been Contentious and Unresolved for Decades. In the Past, Director Zhang had a saying of "70% into the Sea, 30% into the Yangtze." The Huai River Guidance Committee's Plan to Guide the Huai River into the Yangtze Was Based on the Principle of Not Allowing the Yangtze River to Exceed Its Highest Water Level in the Tenth Year of the Republic of China, While Adding an Outlet to the Sea Was Contingent on Future Sufficient Funding (Refer to Section Two of the Huai River Project Plan Published by the Huai River Guidance Committee). An examination of the water level of the Yangtze River this year reveals that it could not be made to exceed the 10th year of the Republic, something that has never occurred since water levels started to be recorded, so the guiding principal of channeling the water into the Yangtze cannot be relied upon. Furthermore, the Yangtze River downstream is affected by tidal influences, and in the Yangzhou area, the Yangtze River, abruptly receiving such a huge amount of water from the Huai River, its impact on areas near the Jinghu area need not be stated. The impact of this year's floods has clearly shown us that the Yangtze River cannot accommodate the Huai River, and the Huai River cannot be reduced, inevitably resulting in both the Yangtze and Huai Rivers suffering harm. Moreover, the Yangtze, Huai, Yellow, and Ji Rivers are the four major rivers of our country, all flowing to the sea. In my opinion, the Huai River should flow into the sea, and the point of entry into the sea should first focus on the area around the Guan River and Haizhou, connecting it to the Longhai Railway to develop the agricultural and industrial areas throughout the Huai River basin. This fundamental water control measure should be based on the facts and not be transferred based on availability of funding. As for the detailed planning of the entry to the sea, it needs to be done by experts. (B) Conscripting Labor and Military Labor Should Be Considered and Compared Simultaneously. The Huai River Committee's plan to enter the river uses the tenth year of the Republic of China as the highest water level of the Yangtze River. This could not have accounted for the surpassing that level. In addition, using the shortest route to save money is also one of the intentions of entering the river. Although the road to the sea can be used by existing waterways, it must be deepened and widened. The length of the route will be three times that of the river entry. Because the amount of soil is large, the cost of labor is huge. This is based on recruitment. Now that the refugees are everywhere, waiting to be fed, if refugees can be conscripted, with labor as relief, the work of digging soil and building embankments is for the farmers, who are accustomed to the work. The people can save themselves with this effort, and work to make sure the Huai River exits on its own forever. This is one way. The military labor policy has been promoted worldwide. Although our country's imitation has not been popularized, it has been effective. Jiangsu Pacification Supervisor Zhang Zhijiang and military commander Liang Guanying have had the same compassionate mindset, and they are stationed in the Huai River Basin. Recently, Liang led his men to dredge the river. If it is possible to organize a military labor force, and use the spirit of bloody battles on the battlefield to compete with the flood, with organization and training, it will be twice as effective with half the effort, and it is also possible to save the cost of labor with wages instead of labor. This is also a way. If the situation can be weighed and properly deployed, labor conscription and military labor can be implemented in sections, so as to compare and encourage each other, the future promotion of waterway management throughout the country will have scale.

▲Five District Relief Commissioners The Disaster Area Work Group of the National Government Relief Committee for Flood Disasters, as announced by General Zhu Qinglan, has dispatched relief commissioners to five important disaster areas (Wuhan District, Jiujiang District, Anqing-Wuhu District, Canal District, and Yuezhou in the Xiang River Basin) to handle all relief matters. The names and brief biographies of the commissioners are outlined below. Li Jin is the relief commissioner for the Wuhan District. Zhang Rujun, president of the Tianjin Red Swastika Society, is handling the Wuhu-Anqing District. Zhou Baipeng, the Shandong commissioner of the China International Famine Relief Commission, is the commissioner for the Jiujiang District. Zhang Peinian is the commissioner for the Canal District (or Jiangbei District). Mr. Zhang, named Xi, has experience in salt reclamation and engineering and is familiar with the water conservancy situation in Jiangbei. Zhao Shouyu is the commissioner for the Yuezhou District. He handled road construction relief work during the Shanxi drought in the sixth, ninth, and tenth years of the Republic of China. All of the above individuals have extensive experience and knowledge and will surely be able to fulfill their duties satisfactorily.

▲Zhou Fu and Feng Sui Suggest Zhou Fu, a citizen of this city, and Feng Sui, a member of the Party, and others submitted a petition to the National Government Relief Committee for Flood Disasters yesterday, advocating for a uniform deduction of 1% of the official interest from all companies nationwide for twenty years to be allocated to relief funds. The original text is as follows: (Omitted above) From our limited perspective, all companies, factories, and merchants nationwide are collective bodies of capital and the center of the nation's economic power. In the face of national crisis, they should rise up with the spirit of the entire nation to provide relief for the entire nation with the nation's power. Furthermore, companies are mostly organized with shares and very few are individually owned. It is better for the majority to bear a small burden than for the minority to bear a large burden. As citizens, we have repeatedly considered proposing that the council submit a bill requiring all companies, factories, and merchants of a commercial nature to deduct 1% of the official interest from the total amount of paid-in capital for the twentieth year, which must be paid in advance within one month. Those with special circumstances in operations who truly have no profits and cannot maintain the official interest should be allowed to submit a statement to the relevant authorities for appropriate reduction or exemption. Based on this calculation, the power of the whole country can easily raise millions. In general, there are several benefits: the funds are taken from the capital side and do not affect the livelihood of workers, which is one benefit; the operations are already profitable, and the loss of one percent of the official interest in one year is minimal, and there is no feeling on the part of the capital side, which is the second benefit; the shares are raised and allocated pro rata, universally and equally, which is the third benefit; when the company issues interest, the official interest is still distributed according to the original regulations, and the deduction of 1% for disaster relief can be used as a receipt to offset, and there is no damage to business reputation, which is the fourth benefit; all formally established companies have government records to check the number of shares, no need to solicit for donations and without uneven burden, which is the fifth benefit. We believe that this method of raising relief funds is more convenient and easier than any design, which is a matter of national survival. We hereby submit this petition to your department, hoping for adoption and implementation, to alleviate the disaster and relieve the people's lives. Aside from submitting to the Shanghai Municipal Party Department, we hereby submit to the National Government Relief Committee for Flood Disasters. Opinion writers: Zhou Fu, Co-signers: Jin Hanzhai, Party members Feng Sui, Wang Huochu, Xu Weimin, You Chengan, Zhang Ziwen, Zhu Jingrong, Tan Zhongguang, Zhuang Zexian, Zhou Mingshan.

The amount of funds is 25,000 yuan for Gaoyou, 20,000 yuan for Xinghua, 10,000 yuan each for Jiangdu, Baoying, Huaiyin, Huai'an, Siyang, Funing, Jiangpu, Tongshan, and Luhe, and 5,000 yuan each for Yangzhou, Jintan, Liyang, and Lianshui, and 3,000 yuan for Ganyu. The above 16 counties will be handled by this association. The total funds for the two associations are 260,000 yuan. However, it is still necessary to wait for the 130,000 yuan allocated by the National Government Relief Committee and the 1 million yuan of construction bonds previously allocated by the provincial government to the association for disaster relief, to mortgage cash with the Shanghai Banking Association, and to release the 130,000 yuan before distribution can be made.

▲Disaster Assessment Report Wang Qijie, Chief of the Document Section of the Association, was dispatched to survey the flood disaster in Baoshan and has returned to Shanghai yesterday. The report is as follows: (1) Pingan Township: The township belongs to Xinsha and has more than 400 households. The entire sand area is about 5,000 to 6,000 mu. This time, the storm surged, and the outer embankments were all broken. Upon inspection, there were many breaches. More than 300 households were destroyed, accounting for 90%. Nine people were drowned. Survivors mostly took refuge on the embankment. Although the water has receded, the crops have been ruined. The few farmland inside the embankments is still being flooded by the morning and afternoon tides due to the breaches not being repaired. It is difficult to expect an autumn harvest, estimated to be no more than 20% to 30%. (2) Ruiyongding Township: The township is a merger of the Ruifeng, Dingxin, and Yongxin sand areas, west of Pingan. It is also a new sand area, with about 7,000 to 8,000 mu of land and more than 500 households. About 30 households in Dingxin. Six people were drowned. The embankments were also breached in many places. The autumn harvest is estimated to be only 30% to 40%. (3) Changxing Township: The township is commonly known as Yawo Sand, east of Pingan. It belongs to the old sand area and is larger in area, with about 10,000 to several thousand mu of farmland and about 1,100 households. 105 households were destroyed by the storm surge. The Dongxing Sand area, which belongs to it, is low-lying, and the collapse is even more severe. 11 people were drowned. There are 34 embankments in the entire township. Except for the inner Zeng and inner Fu embankments, which were fortunately not affected, the destruction of the Zengkang 2357 De and other embankments was quite severe. If they can be repaired separately, the autumn harvest may be 40% to 50%. (4) Shidong Township: The township is north of Ruiyongding, with a smaller area, about 100 to 200 households, and more than 3,000 mu of farmland. The collapse of embankments and houses was quite damaging, but fortunately, there were not many. If the embankments are repaired early, the autumn harvest is expected to be 50% to 60%. Of the above four townships, Pingan was the most severely affected, followed by the others. Looking from above, there are few households. The thatch between the embankments is several feet deep, all of which are tenant houses, scattered by the storm surge. Currently, the owners are mostly waiting and seeing due to the high cost of repairing the embankments. Not only is there no harvest, but it is also difficult to plant wheat. These displaced tenant farmers have no way to find food, and their livelihoods are in despair. It seems that relief should be given from the relief funds.

▲China International Famine Relief Commission Relief Meeting The China International Famine Relief Commission held a board meeting at 5:00 PM the day before yesterday to discuss the relief of the flood disaster in Jiangbei.

▲Report by Vice President Gu Vice President Gu Jisheng reported that he and Lu Bohong and Wang Junsheng went to Yangzhou to organize a local branch and start relief efforts. After arriving in Yangzhou, they contacted the president and vice president of the local Chamber of Commerce, as well as Li Siduo of the Xinghua Catholic Church and Peng Siduo of Dongtai, to organize the branch. All parties welcomed the work of the association. It was decided to organize the Yangzhou branch immediately. The victims in the disaster area of Yangzhou had no food or clothing, and the situation was extremely miserable. Xinghua looked like the bottom of a cauldron, and the disaster was the most serious. At present, there are many charitable organizations starting emergency relief, but the most important thing to pay attention to is the preparation for winter relief. Because the flood came suddenly, the victims were able to escape, but most of them escaped in single clothes, and some were naked. Because the weather was still hot at that time. Now that the weather is getting colder, and the west wind is blowing, the victims will freeze to death without clothing. It is urgent to prepare relief clothing. Because it takes time to make clothes, it takes time to transport clothes, and it takes time to distribute them. It is not too early to prepare now. Therefore, all parties hope that the association will pay attention to this, and ask for discussion and resolution on how to handle it.

▲Resolution on the Distribution of Relief Funds The funds that the association has already allocated for emergency relief in Jiangbei include 10,000 yuan for Yancheng, 10,000 yuan for Taizhou, 8,000 yuan for Xinghua, 10,000 yuan for Yangzhou, and 5,000 yuan for Qingjiangpu and Huai'an. Now that the Yangzhou branch is organized, it is decided to allocate another 30,000 yuan and invite Li Siduo of Xinghua and Peng Siduo of Dongtai to join the Yangzhou branch to handle the distribution. As for cotton clothing, it was previously decided to make 10,000 sets, which is a drop in the bucket. It was decided to make another 20,000 sets to avoid digging a well when thirsty. Furthermore, the Hunan Association in Shanghai sent a letter stating that the province's flood disaster affected 54 counties, requesting an allocation of funds. It was decided to allocate 5,000 yuan for emergency use by the association.

If we do not plan comprehensively, we fear that we will be exhausted in providing relief. We look forward to the future with trepidation.
