Wen Zhi and Wen Chuan are getting old, but we dare not complain about the efforts for the sake of good deeds. This year's flood has swept across the country, and Wuxi has also been hit by a silkworm famine. The homes in the four villages are all hanging upside down. We must help others and help ourselves. Our hearts are long and our strength is short, and we are deeply afraid that we will not be able to bear the burden. We ask you to give us advice and assistance at any time. In addition to waiting for the donation books of this association to be printed and sent for your review, we also hope to give advice. Tang Wenzhi, President of the Wuxi Flood Relief Committee, and Hua Yishan, Vice President, kowtow. The association has replied separately by telegram, continuing to raise relief funds. Continued Reports of Disaster Situation in Various Counties of Anhui 113

▲ In Quanjiao, flash floods occurred, drowning countless people and livestock. Dikes and embankments were completely turned into swamps, and the number of houses that collapsed is incalculable.

▲ In Hanshan, more than sixty embankments across the county, totaling over one hundred li, were all breached. The number of houses and livestock swept away is countless. Hundreds of thousands of survivors are naked in the water, without clothing, food, or shelter. Their cries of hunger and cold are unbearable to hear.

▲ In Hefei, flash floods occurred, and the city and countryside were completely turned into swamps. Dikes and embankments were all destroyed, and fields and houses were swept away without a trace. The number of people and livestock who died is incalculable.

▲ In Lujiang, flash floods occurred, and more than seventy embankments along the river successively collapsed. Even high-lying cultivated fields were submerged. The entire area is a vast expanse of water, and people and livestock were swept away. Those who did not die in the water also lack clothing and food.

▲ In Tongcheng, the river rose sharply and embankments collapsed. Houses were barely visible above the water, and the number of people and livestock drowned is even harder to count. In Chenjia Island alone, there are already 40,000 displaced people. The disaster situation in Qingcaogema in the western countryside is even more dire.

▲ In Dangtu, flash floods occurred. A total of 370-380 large and small embankments, totaling 600,000 mu, were completely submerged. Houses collapsed, and people and livestock were drowned. 300,000 disaster victims are sleeping in the open air, exposed to wind and rain, their faces emaciated and their bodies gaunt, a truly unbearable sight.

Japanese Ships Refuse Chinese Passengers to Japan Under Pretext of Epidemic Prevention 116

Since Japan recognized Shanghai as a port with an epidemic, it has required all passengers going to Japan from Shanghai to be tested for feces. Recently, under the pretext of epidemic testing, it has refused to sell ship tickets to Chinese people, effectively preventing Chinese people from going abroad. The details are as follows:

▲ Japanese Postal Company Stops Selling Ship Tickets The Japanese Postal Company has now received an order from its headquarters, citing epidemic prevention reasons, to stop selling ship tickets to Chinese passengers going to Yokohama from Shanghai. The reason is to prevent the spread of epidemics, but in reality, it is to prevent Chinese third-class passengers from going to that port. Therefore, Chinese people who have recently purchased passenger tickets to land at Yokohama from Japanese shipping companies have been refused.

▲ Japanese Mail Ships Prohibit Chinese Passengers Japanese mail ships traveling from Shanghai to the Orient include European and American routes. It has now been decided that for any Chinese people going to Japan, except for ships specifically sailing between China and Japan, those who have booked third-class seats on various mail ships will not be allowed to board. This prohibition on Chinese people buying mail ship tickets has already begun.

Determines Five-Year Industry Plan

The Anti-Japanese Design Association held its sixth committee meeting yesterday at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's regular meeting room. Li Wenjie chaired, and Secretary Xue Guangqian recorded. After reporting matters, the following resolutions were made: (1) Discussing the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's letter stating that the methods prescribed in the council's resolution on disposing of Japanese goods are particularly difficult, and requesting that more appropriate and quick methods be devised. It was resolved that, according to the original intention of the methods, scattered goods were not included in the list of goods to be stored in warehouses. (2) Discussing Committee Member Que Pingzhi's proposal to urge industrial factories to intensify production in order to implement the goal of permanent boycott. It was resolved to adopt and implement it. (3) Discussing the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce's letter transferring three opinions of the Chinese Cereals and Oil Cake Industry Association on resisting Japanese goods. (2) Resolved: (1) Foreign goods handled by Japanese merchants are absolutely boycotted. It was decided that foreign goods should avoid being transported by Japanese ships or stored in Japanese warehouses as much as possible. (3) Domestic goods can be freely exported. It was also decided that the five-year industry plan is of great importance to China's future, and it is not enough to establish a long-term plan without gathering experts from all over the country to discuss it at length. The association should wait for the establishment of the National Anti-Japanese Association, and then jointly discuss the steps to be taken to draft it, in order to collect opinions from all sides and avoid omissions.

Jiangsu Construction Department Issues Instructions to Investigate and Report on Disaster Situation 120

The Jiangsu Construction Department yesterday ordered the county construction bureaus, stating: "In order to comply, it is found that this summer, there has been continuous rainfall, and the amount of rainfall has been particularly high, resulting in rivers overflowing and dikes collapsing. The severity of the disaster in the province is rare in recent years. Recently, many counties have reported on the flood situation and requested methods for relief, but they are all briefly mentioned without detailed information. For both symptomatic and fundamental solutions, and to plan for relief, it is necessary to investigate and clarify the flood situation in all counties of the province to facilitate overall planning. In addition to distributing, a flood investigation form has been formulated and is attached. You are required to comply, fill in each item in detail, and report back as soon as possible. These are the instructions. Details are as follows: Matters to be investigated and reported: (Rainfall) Total rainfall for July and August, rainfall on the day with the greatest heavy rain. (Flood situation) Cause of the disaster, area affected, which area is most severely affected, degree of damage to fields and crops, number of dike breaches and length of damaged dikes, condition of damaged gates and dikes, number of people drowned, situation of people displaced, other losses (Rescue situation) Number of dike repairmen, number of gate repairs, number of dike repairs (Relief methods) Current relief methods, fundamental solutions."

National Chamber of Commerce Cables to Request the Prohibition of Illegal Taxation at Aigun Customs 121

The All-China Federation of Chambers of Commerce cabled the Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, and Ministry of Industry of the National Government yesterday, stating: "We recently received a letter from the Aigun-Heihe Chamber of Commerce in Heilongjiang, stating: 'The establishment of customs is originally a taxation authority for foreign countries, and its taxation scope is limited to exports and imports. The so-called exports and imports refer to international trade, not that it is an export just by going in and out of the local area. However, Aigun Customs (stationed in Heihe) does not ask whether the goods are entering or leaving Chinese ports, and taxes them all uniformly. Even goods traveling back and forth between Heihe and Harbin that have already been taxed cannot escape the example of repeated taxation. Such collection, similar to likin, is obviously inconsistent with the principle of one tax per item. Furthermore, the taxation of Aigun Customs is purely limited to river transportation, while goods coming and going by land are ignored. We think that the transportation of goods by river and land are both within the scope of Heihe, so why is river transportation taxed, while land transportation is uniquely exempt from taxation? Such unfairness will inevitably drive merchants to land routes. Furthermore, the taxation of Manzhouli and Suifenhe Customs is limited to exported goods only, otherwise they are exempt. Why is Aigun Customs the opposite of this principle? At a time when customs autonomy is being implemented and likin is being abolished, our country's industries and the south should implement protection policies to resist foreign merchants. Unexpectedly, commercial decline and deterioration are inevitable in all places where customs are established. For example, in the remote Sanxing, commerce has become increasingly prosperous and the locality has gradually flourished since the abolition of customs. It is conceivable whether customs are harmful to the people. Heihe is now in the same situation as Sanxing before the abolition of customs. If we do not provide relief soon, I am afraid there will never be a day of recovery. Therefore, we implore your association to quickly forward this request to the central management authorities to correct this situation as soon as possible to benefit merchants and the people.' Upon receiving this, we found that customs taxation has its own regulations. If it is as stated by the association, it will inevitably violate the law, harm merchants, and hinder business. It is reasonable to cable your government departments for inspection. We earnestly implore you to quickly order correction to relieve merchants in difficulty. Chairman Lin Kanghou of the All-China Federation of Chambers of Commerce, Standing Committee Members Su Minsheng, Zhang Yuquan, Lu Guangji, Chen Riping, Li Kuian, and Peng Chuli, bow. Yang Yin."

Zheng Yuanxing Talks About Egg Product Registration Rules 122

The Management Rules for Foreign Trade Registration of Egg Products, drafted by the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, have been submitted to the Ministry of Industry for promulgation and implementation. A Shanghai press reporter visited Mr. Zheng Yuanxing, Chairman of the Shanghai Egg Industry Association, yesterday to ask for his opinion on the rules. The following is an excerpt from his conversation: (Question) According to the Management Rules for Foreign Trade Registration of Egg Products, it is necessary to obtain guarantees from two reputable businesses in the same industry. Do you feel that this is inconvenient for your industry? (Answer) Since the implementation of these registration rules, there has been no inconvenience to our industry. Because there are not many businesses in our industry, and there is considerable contact due to foreign relations, we all know each other's financial strength, credit, experience, and products. Therefore, obtaining guarantees from businesses in the same industry is easier than obtaining guarantees from other industries. (Question) Egg products should be reported for inspection when exported. If the Inspection Bureau inspects carefully, inferior goods cannot be exported by obfuscation. Why is it necessary to obtain guarantees from businesses in the same industry? (Answer) Inspecting egg products is different from inspecting other goods. If export manufacturers, in the event of unavoidable circumstances, intentionally take chances and occasionally try, then no matter how strict the inspection is, it is impossible to prevent it. The case reported in the Chinese and foreign newspapers this year, where a certain company was sued in court after being discovered by a foreign buyer for mixing water into eggs and exporting them, can serve as clear proof. As far as I can see, the reason why the rules require guarantees from businesses in the same industry is because the Inspection Bureau cannot supervise everything, and wants to use mutual supervision among businesses in the same industry to prevent problems before they arise. (Question) Have all Chinese and foreign egg exporters completely complied with the current registration requirements? (Answer) As far as I know, they have all complied. (Question) Can you guarantee that egg exports will be completely good in the future and avoid foreign excuses? (Answer) If the Ministry of Industry can insist on obtaining guarantees from two reputable businesses in the same industry for the registration of export eggs by commodity inspection bureaus across the country, foreign excuses can be avoided. At this point, Mr. Zheng solemnly said to the reporter, "In recent years, competition in the international market for egg products has been extremely fierce. Our egg industry colleagues must be of one heart and one mind, and strive for the excellence of goods and the balance of prices. Even a slight carelessness will give our enemies excellent propaganda material, and put our industry in a situation from which it cannot recover. It is chilling to think about. Therefore, our industry should be vigilant and do well on its own, without waiting for government supervision." He then excused himself and left.

Taxpayers' Association Discusses the Text Format of Water Bills 126

Directly Stopping Water Supply to Residents is Not Allowed

The Taxpayers' Association sent a letter to the British-owned Shanghai Water Company, stating: "To Whom It May Concern: We have received your letter of September 5 regarding the addition of Chinese text on water bills, and the sample bill you attached. We are very impressed with your company's respect for Chinese opinions. However, after reviewing it, we feel that the format of the bill receipt is still difficult to understand, as the method of arranging Chinese and English is completely different. For example, the item of silver number is still recorded in Arabic numerals, which may not be entirely appropriate. Furthermore, 'water supply contract (No.)' is even more incomprehensible. It may be better to change it to 'water supply according to the contract,' which seems clearer. The phrase 'small foreign money (or auxiliary currency) according to the city's exchange rate' is more common. Adding the word 'calculation' makes it awkward. The following is what this association would like your company to pay special attention to, that is, the layer of water outage for non-payment of water bill. This association believes that at least it should follow the method of non-payment of rent (and the rented house is not a patent, and the landlord cannot directly stop renting the house). However, for the patented water, and those who have no substitutes available, and without legal procedures to stop the direct action of supply, there are many abuses. This association believes that there should be room for detailed consideration, and the excessive discrepancy in the phrase 'or its predecessor' should also be removed. According to this association's opinion, if it is changed to 'If this account is not paid by ○ month 28, the company may handle it according to law,' it would be more legal and reasonable. A corresponding letter is sent to you, and we hope that you will check and handle it."

Amicable Resolution in the Da Lun Case 133

Five Conditions Stipulated

Tenants Given a Fixed Time to Vacate

The buildings at Zhifu Lane near the Nanjing Road and Fujian Road intersection are the property of the Da Lun Real Estate Company. Previously, due to the establishment of the Great China Department Store, the company intended to rebuild a seven-story building and notified all tenants, including Lao Da Fang and Chang Feng Hang, to relocate. This resulted in a lawsuit in the First Special District Court. The initial trial resulted in a loss for the landlord. Da Lun Company, dissatisfied with the verdict, appealed. The Court of Appeal sent the case back to the original court for retrial. It is now heard that the attorneys for the appellant, Li Zuyu and Qin Liankui, and the attorney for the appellee, Wang Youling, repeatedly negotiated an amicable resolution. A settlement agreement was reached, and a request was made to the First Special District Court to close the case. Yesterday, Judge Li Mo held a hearing. The attorneys for both parties explained the terms of the settlement. Five conditions were stipulated: (1) Due to the difficulty for the tenants to relocate immediately, the landlord allows the tenants an extension to relocate, with two years and four months from September of this year as the final relocation period. Regardless of any reason, they must relocate by that time. The landlord will also have the right to demolish or reclaim the property at that time. (2) During the extension period, the tenants will continue to pay rent at the original rate, paying in advance and not delaying. (3) The previously owed rent (more than ten months) must be paid in a lump sum for eight months, with the remaining amount paid one month at a time until cleared. (4) If any of the above conditions are violated, immediate relocation is required. (5) The litigation costs will be borne by the plaintiff and defendant respectively, and a request to close the case was made. Thus, a property dispute case came to an end.

Zhu Yunqing Kidnapped Yesterday 134

A car was parked at the gate of Zhen He Tea House, No. 173, Lane 6, De'an Lane, North Shanxi Road, Zhengjia Mu Bridge, French Concession. The tea house is owned by the wealthy merchant Zhu Baoyuan. It has been in operation for many years and has accumulated considerable wealth, making it a target for kidnappers. His third son, named Yunqing, lives separately at No. 94 in the lane next to the Republican Theater on Fangbang Bridge in the South City. Every morning around 7:00 a.m., he takes his private car to the Zhen He Tea House to work, returning home only after 11:00 p.m. It has become a habit. Yesterday evening at 11:30 p.m., the chauffeur, Chen Zhengfu from Zhenjiang, was driving him back south when they arrived at the iron gate of Zheng Mu Bridge in the French Concession. A covered car was parked on the side of the road, facing north, license number 10009. Three people were sitting in the car. Upon seeing Zhu's car, two people jumped out, drew handguns, and prohibited any outcry. They forced Zhu Yunqing into the car, and the kidnapper driver sped south. The chauffeur, Chen Zhengfu, was so frightened by the sight that he stood frozen like a wooden chicken. Only after the car had gone far did he shout loudly for the police to come. He accompanied the police to the Grand Self-Ringing Bell Police Station to report the incident. The police chief immediately ordered Chinese and Western detectives to rush out to search, but the kidnapping was already like chasing a yellow crane. Later, Chen Zhengfu returned home and reported the kidnapping to the mistress of the house.

Swindled of 100,000 Yuan in Government Bonds 135

Impersonating the Wenzhou Fuzi Qianzhuang

Defrauding the Shanghai Tongyi Company

The Wenzhou Fuzi Qianzhuang has had dealings with the Tongyi Trust Company at No. 126 Beijing Road, Shanghai. On the 31st of last month, the Tongyi Company suddenly received an urgent letter from the Fuzi Qianzhuang, stating that Zhu Ming was being sent to deliver 100,000 yuan in Post-Reorganization and Disbandment Government Bonds, and requesting them to hand them over to him to take down. The letter was prominently stamped with the Fuzi Qianzhuang's seal and the manager's chop. Soon after, Zhu Ming arrived with a letter from the Fuzi Qianzhuang to collect the government bonds. The company handed them over in full, and Zhu left with them. In the afternoon, Tongyi suddenly received a telegram from the Fuzi Qianzhuang, stating that the bank's seal had been lost, and that if anyone came to collect anything, they should refuse to hand it over. Tongyi was greatly alarmed and immediately telegraphed Fuzi, informing them that someone had already taken 100,000 yuan in government bonds. The Fuzi Qianzhuang then sent staff to Shanghai and investigations revealed that Dai Dingfu of Hangzhou was deeply involved in the case. They reported this to the Hangzhou Public Security Bureau's Detective Team, who arrested Dai. At the same time, Xu Bohua was also arrested. Xu was released after questioning revealed he was not involved, while Dai confessed that Zeng Liulin and Zhu Xiang (who claimed to be Zhu Ming) were the main culprits. He said that Zeng lived in Room 511 of the East Asia Hotel in Shanghai. The Tongyi Company reported this to the General Police Station on the previous day, and detectives Liu Xiangzhai and others were ordered to go to Room 511 of the East Asia Hotel, where they arrested Zhao Luoshu, Chen Susheng, and Chen Yaoyao. Xu Bohua was also in the room and was arrested along with them. However, Zeng Liulin had already fled after hearing the news. Zhao and the other three were taken to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Summary Court of the First Special Court. The police lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, explained the case and stated that it was not yet clear whether Zhao and the other three were involved in the case, so the police were not prosecuting them. He only requested that they be temporarily detained for further investigation. Judge Jiang Gongliang reviewed the report and questioned Zhao Luoshu and the others, then ordered that they be temporarily detained.

Large-Scale Theft of Valuable Woolen Cloth from German Ship 136

Sixteen People Involved Arrested

Court Held a Preliminary Hearing Yesterday

On the morning of the 24th of last month, at 2:30 a.m., forty-two pieces of woolen cloth worth over 10,000 taels of silver were stolen from the German merchant ship "Bowness", which was docked at the China Merchants Bureau's North Machinery Wharf. On the previous day, the Water Police, together with Chinese detectives Liu Baoshan, Chen Ruhai, and Xu Yongyuan from the Huishan Police Station, and Russian detectives, arrested sixteen suspects, including Tang Xiaohangzi, Han Ke, Shang Wei, and Zhou Zhihe, at various locations including Broadway Road, Fuzhou Road, the Shangxian Hotel, Xizang Road, Nanjing Road, and Route Tenant de la Tour in the French Concession. All the stolen goods were recovered, along with 800 yuan in silver notes that Zhou Zhihe had stored at the Shangxian Hotel. All were taken to the police station and detained. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special Court. The police lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, presented the case, stating that the recovered woolen cloth had not been taxed by customs. Now, the Customs Service has a letter stating that the cloth should be inspected by customs. If no original owner claims it, it will be considered tax evasion and will belong to the state. Therefore, Bai Liqi, a Western officer representing the Water Police, was sent to the court and presented the letter. Then, the Chinese and Western detectives explained the circumstances of the arrests and handed over the seized original woolen cloth and silver notes. Bai Liqi, the Western officer of the Water Police, requested that the woolen cloth be taken back to customs for safekeeping. When Tang Xiaohangzi was questioned, he claimed that he knew nothing about the theft from the ship and had been mistakenly arrested. Detective Liu of the police station stated that his statement was false and that he had identified Yuan Da, Zhang Xiaozhang, Chen Erxi, Chen Erbianzi, and others. Han Ke stated that he was a dockworker and had been invited by Li Jinyu to help unload goods for a reward. Later, he was arrested at the Shangxian Hotel. Shang Wei gave a similar statement. Yuan Da also stated that he was a dockworker and had been invited by Li to move cloth and load it onto a barge, receiving ten yuan. Zhang Xiaozhang stated that he was selling beer on the ship when he saw many people moving cloth. He was given seventeen yuan by Li and told not to make a sound. Shang Liexi, Zhu Xiaokouzi, Zhong Xiaosheng, Chen Erxi, and Chen Erbianzi all stated that they were dockworkers and had been invited by Li to be lookouts on the ship, each receiving five yuan. Liu Jinbo stated that he was arrested while going to Shang Lie's place to collect rent. Zhou Zhihe stated that he was a foreign goods broker and Li Jinyu had asked him to sell the woolen cloth, saying it was water-damaged goods from Hankou, or to use it as collateral. He then entrusted Dai Junji to sell it on his behalf. When questioned, Dai admitted that he was entrusted by Zhou to take the goods to his relative Zhu Xinyang to sell, but they were not needed and were used as collateral for 4,725.40 taels of silver. He did not know that the goods were stolen and he and Zhou only earned a small commission. Chen Xinsheng stated that he and Zhou Zhihe were at the Changle Teahouse on Fuzhou Road when Li Jinyu asked him to sell the woolen cloth, and he entrusted it to Zhou Zhihe, knowing that it was water-damaged goods from Hankou. If he could sell it, he would earn some commission. Han Lide stated that he was an employee at a native goods store at the Xinqiao Tou in the West Gate. He happened to be at Zhang Xiaozhang's place to collect money when he was mistakenly arrested. Zhu Xinyang stated that he was harmed by his relative Dai Junji, who forced him to take twenty-four pieces of the woolen cloth as collateral. At the time, he asked in detail whether the goods were reliable. He guaranteed that they would not cause any trouble and that they were definitely water-damaged goods from Hankou, which is why he paid the silver. The price was almost the same as the market price. He hired two lawyers, Wu Linkun and Wang Fuchang, to request bail. Judge Shen Bingrong ordered that all be remanded except for those who provided reliable shopkeepers as guarantors, and adjourned the hearing. The stolen goods were temporarily taken away by the Jianghai Customs.

(2) Boat Crew: Zhang Awei, a local, over fifty years old, was a boatman since childhood. He is currently working on the Taikoo Company's No. 4 barge. He is addicted to alcohol and always gets drunk. Friends and relatives have repeatedly advised him to stop, but he does not listen. At 10:00 PM the night before last, he bought wine and drank heavily again, until he was completely drunk. Everyone advised him to go ashore and go home, but he refused and fell asleep on the boat, snoring loudly. He accidentally rolled over and fell into the river. By the time his fellow crew members noticed, Zhang had already sunk to the bottom of the river and could not be rescued. Reader Correspondence

Message from Mr. Ye Jingxin

The most important question is the future of university students. What puzzles me is that Chinese universities only teach people to be active within the school. Once they graduate, they truly "graduate," not only from their university studies but also from any potential career in society. Naturally, everyone is shouting, "There's nothing to do!" and complaining, "Can't find a job!" Are there no unfinished tasks in the world? Are there no remaining careers waiting for someone to pursue? Social scholars wearing their glasses can understand the crux of the matter and express sympathy, pitying the unemployed students, or even shouting a few words of encouragement. However, the friends who were about to secure a position but suddenly had the offer rescinded and are now unemployed continue to write numerous articles asking "What should we do?" that remain on paper. I sincerely seek a solution from the reporter, a practical way to provide university students with a path forward. Please answer this public concern in the newspaper.

(Reply) The problem probably doesn't lie solely after graduation but largely in the university education itself. It involves the issues before students enter university and during their studies, and partly the economic recession.

The economic recession involves too many aspects to discuss for now.

As far as we know, there is currently a shortage of engineering talents and medical professionals. Even notices are posted seeking certain experts, but no one applies. This shows that society doesn't lack a need for talent, but the talents being cultivated don't match the demand. This is something that university departments and students should pay attention to early on.

Furthermore, the teaching方針 and methods of universities and the attitude of university students towards their studies are also connected to the issue of future career paths. This also deserves attention.

For now, let's focus solely on solving the difficulty of finding employment after graduation.

The difficulty in finding employment mainly involves seeking jobs from others. Since seeking jobs from others is ineffective, let's think about seeking our own way. For example, several like-minded people could collaborate on writing or translating books. We know selling manuscripts is very difficult and frustrating. However, I believe that if the selected topics are indeed needed by society, or if it's a translation, send the original book or a trial translation to the purchasing organization for review. If it truly moves them, they will definitely be happy to accept it. This method can also enhance one's own knowledge. This is just an example, and there might be similar methods.

However, not all university graduates have this kind of ability. Let's discuss two nearly passive methods first. I hope that university graduates can discard their sense of status and various preconceived notions, analyze their difficult situation, and then find a solution.

(1) Half of the reason for not finding a job is probably due to the wrong major, which is truly unchangeable. One can only study a more socially needed subject in the short term.

(2) Half of the reason for not finding a job might be the lack of positions equivalent to a university degree. This is truly unchangeable. One can only take a step back and think again, and if there is nothing, take another step back.

I think that most university students are reluctant to accept these two points. However, I have already stated that these are solutions when there is no other way. It is best to solve the problem from the root, as mentioned earlier, before teaching and before studying.

The above is for university students to consider themselves. I sincerely hope that the government and social leaders can come up with a plan as soon as possible to absorb a large number of university graduates, so that they don't wander aimlessly for a long time.

Shanghai Daily Reader Communication Regulations 155

The contributors to this newspaper firmly believe that the readers each have certain pressing issues that urgently need discussion. Based on the spirit of serving society, the contributors are willing to act as consultants, with the utmost sincerity, to engage in textual discussions. If readers can obtain appropriate solutions as a result, alleviate some difficulties, and increase some happiness, how delightful it would be!

1. The issues that readers wish to discuss with the contributors of this newspaper are temporarily limited to the three categories of education, career, and marriage.

2. When communicating, please first state your full name, gender, age, occupation (or place of study, grade), native place, and mailing address (it is still advisable to provide detailed information when continuing communication, as we fear that previous letters may not have been received). Then, start a new paragraph and state the issue you wish to discuss. The text should be detailed, accurate, and easy to understand. Please write "Shanghai Daily Reader Communication Department" on the outside of the envelope and attach sufficient postage for a reply.

3. When communicating, you must cut out the special printed stamp from the Shanghai Daily Reader Communication section and paste it in the upper left corner of the stationery as a voucher.

4. The handling method after this newspaper receives the letter: A. Respect the reader's wishes. All letters stating that they wish not to be answered in the newspaper or that they do not wish their names to be disclosed when answering will be complied with. B. Letters that do not state how they wish to be answered, but which the contributors believe that answering one person will provide reference value for everyone, will be disclosed in the newspaper.

However, if the letter states that it wishes to be answered in the newspaper, but is limited by space, only selected excerpts will be disclosed, or even not disclosed, or because the issue is still under consideration, it will have to be disclosed later, please forgive us. However, if it cannot be answered in the newspaper, it will still be answered by mail.

Free Talk

Not Removing the Garden Grass Zhai Fu Talk Collection

Tian Shan Tiger 173

The tigers I have seen in my life are only tigers on paper, tigers on the screen, and tigers in cages. I regret that I have not seen tigers in the mountains, and I have repeatedly wanted to draw the tiger in my heart to express my thoughts of the mountain tiger. The ancients said: (Drawing a tiger unsuccessfully, instead resembles a dog.) My tiger painting is not successful, but it looks like a cat and not a dog. Now I give up tiger paintings and write tiger poems, I wonder if it looks like a poetry cat.

(Look at the Tian Shan tiger, solemn and majestic. A roar shakes the heaven and earth; a raging wind chases the rain. Wild nature has not been eliminated, the forest can be self-entertained. Sleeps on the cliff of the mountain in the evening; swims on the shore of the water in the morning. Likes to listen to birds singing, all beasts dance to it. Does not harm people when full; swallows water buffalo when hungry. Once passed through Huansha Creek; does not change the Huansha girl. Returns under the bright moon. Lies facing the white clouds and speaks.

Record of Lu Haodong of the First Guangzhou Uprising 174

— Zizai

After the establishment of the Revive China Society, Sun Yat-sen, Chen Shaobai, Yang Quyun, Lu Haodong and others strived for the anti-Qing movement, plotting to seize Guangzhou as a base. After half a year of preparation, they launched the uprising on September 9th. This was in the year 17 before the founding of the Republic of China, the year of Yì Wèi. It was the first uprising of Premier Sun's revolution. Unfortunately, it failed. Qiu Si, Zhu Guiquan, Lu Haodong, Cheng Yaochen, and others were martyred as a result. At that time, the Governor-General of Guangdong was Tan Zhonglin (father of Tan Zuan). Considering the importance of the matter, he specially ordered the magistrates of Nanhai and Panyu counties to conduct strict interrogations, intending to use this opportunity to launch a large-scale crackdown on party members. Li Zhengyong, the magistrate of Nanhai County, brought Lu Haodong in for interrogation, using harsh words and a stern demeanor, ordering Lu to kneel. Lu refused to submit, speaking with generosity and vigor. He requested paper and pen to make a confession, and with a flourish of his pen, he wrote it in one go. His words were: "My surname is Lu, my name is Zhonggui, my alias is Haodong. I am from Cuiwei Township, Xiangshan. I am twenty-nine years old. I have been living outside and have just returned to Guangdong. Together with my fellow villager Sun Wen, I am angered by the corruption and autocracy of the foreign government, the greed and incompetence of officials, and the conspiracies and spying of foreigners. Surveying the Central Plains, it is filled with thorns. Every time I think of it, I truly do not know where my tears should come from." (Omitted) "Helplessly, greedy officials and corrupt gentry, shameless and cowardly, willingly serve the enemy, saying either that the current dynasty has deep benevolence and generous kindness, or that we are scholars who eat the dynasty's grain. How can they know that the Manchus, as a rebellious Jurchen race, entered China, seized our land, killed our ancestors, and plundered our children, women, and treasures? Consider who eats whose grain and who serves whom? The Ten Days of Yangzhou, the Three Massacres of Jiading, and the history of the two princes entering Guangdong and massacring our Han people are well known. And they call this benevolence? In short, today, unless the Qing dynasty is abolished, there is absolutely no way to restore the Han people. Unless traitors are eliminated, there is no way to destroy the Qing dynasty. Therefore, we especially want to kill one or two dog officials as a warning to our Han people. Although the matter has not succeeded, I am very gratified. My words are finished. Please execute me quickly," and so on.

After reading it, Li Zheng was extremely ashamed and fearful of the radical wording of Lu's confession. However, Lu refused to reveal his accomplices, so he used various illegal and cruel tortures, such as nailing and inserting into hands and feet, chiseling teeth, whipping and flogging the back, etc., all of which were exhausted. The cruelty was extreme. He fainted several times, but he firmly refused to confess and regarded death as homecoming, saying to Li: "You dog officials, even if you inflict extreme punishments on me, although my body is in pain, my heart is at peace. What can you do to me?" The next day, the American consul in Guangzhou personally visited Li, saying that Lu was a telegraph translator and not a rebel. He could guarantee it. Li showed him Lu's confession. The American consul left without a word. When Li carried out Tan's order to execute Zhu, Qiu, Lu, and Cheng, Li saw that Lu was young and handsome, and also proficient in literature, so on the day of the execution, he ordered people to dress him in a long gown.

In this battle, Premier Sun first went to Macau and then to Hong Kong. Shi, together with Chen Shaobai and Zheng Shiliang, crossed to Japan. Yang Quyun went to India and various parts of Africa. The rest also hid in Hong Kong and Macau, secretly plotting and striving for a resurgence. Today is the anniversary of the first Guangzhou uprising in the year of Yì Wèi, so we trace and record it.

World Snippets 175

An Unusual Fish in America: Professor C.H. Green of the University of Missouri claims that in 1924, several scientists discovered a peculiar fish in Monterey Bay, California. Its body is covered with hundreds of luminous scales that shimmer and glow. What's particularly interesting is that they emit a sonar-like sound when chasing smaller fish for food, just like humans chasing each other. The world is truly full of wonders.

▲ A Duck Worth 1,000 Pounds: One thousand pounds, calculated at the current price of gold, is equivalent to over 20,000 Mexican silver dollars. To buy a small duck for such a huge sum is astounding, isn't it? However, this is a true event. It is said that this duck was displayed at an exposition in England. It is a Labrador duck. Originally, there were forty-five similar species, found on the northeastern coast of America. Seven years ago, they mysteriously disappeared and became extinct. This duck is the only surviving specimen, hence the price of 1,000 pounds. (Sea Guest)

Zhu Ziqiao, The One Who Has No Time To Warm His Seat 176

— Sun Choucheng

Zhu Ziqiao (Qinglan), a member of the National Government's Relief Committee, is from Shaoxing, Zhejiang. Because he has been away from his hometown for a long time, he cannot speak the Shaoxing dialect. He is very shrewd and quite incorruptible. When he was in office, his political achievements in Guangdong and other places were very good. In recent years, he has abandoned his political career and devoted himself to charitable causes. He has been to Shaanxi four times and Gansu once. His experience in disaster relief is growing day by day. Therefore, the Shanghai community initiated the Emergency Relief Association for the floods in various provinces, inviting him to serve as a standing committee member. The National Government's Flood Relief Committee invited him to serve as a member and also as the director of operations, sending telegrams to invite him to come south. After arriving in Shanghai, he immediately flew to Hankou to inspect the disaster situation. After returning to Shanghai, he flew to northern Jiangsu to look down at the disaster area (bird's-eye view from the plane, without landing). On the one hand, he telegraphed experienced disaster relief workers in North China to come to Shanghai to assist him. On the other hand, he drafted an outline of disaster relief work, focusing on saving lives as a prerequisite and not stopping at saving lives, cultivating the vitality of the people, and restoring the people's ability to produce, treating both the symptoms and the root causes, and using the victims to assist in the implementation of the work, in order to arouse the people's interest in agricultural restoration. Divided into three stages: emergency relief, transition, and recovery, divided into categories and well-organized. If it can be done one by one, it will not only be a blessing for the victims, but also a blessing for the country. Zhu is currently staying at the Yipinxian Hotel on Tibet Road. He gets up very early, reviewing incoming letters and telegrams in the early morning. After ten o'clock, he goes to meetings to work or goes door-to-door to wealthy households to beg for alms, appealing for the victims. All circles admire his enthusiasm and admire his integrity. When others go to solicit donations, nine out of ten doors remain closed. When Mr. Zhu goes, people generously donate. For example, a certain lady had ten thousand yuan in foreign currency, planning to donate it to charity. She had been saving it for a long time, but hesitated because she had no one she trusted. Recently, she heard that Mr. Zhu had come to Shanghai, so she personally sent it to him. His prestige is so moving. He usually advocates vegetarianism, so when Shanghai friends invite him to dinner, it is either at the Jue Lin or the Gongde Lin restaurant. After being seated, he orders a dish or two, then urges the rice to come. His appetite is quite good, able to eat four or five small bowls. Sometimes he drafts telegrams at the banquet. He is nearly sixty years old, full of energy, and has a strong interest in conversation. When he is free in the evening, relatives and friends visit him, and he talks about the past, tirelessly, not leaving until midnight. His hair is already gray, but he has not yet shaved it. When he sees people of his age with beards, such as Wen Lan Ting, Ha Shao Fu, Gu Yanqing, and Xu Shiying, he says (you are a senior, I am a young man). He is physically strong and of great stature. Although he has lived outside the pass for a long time, he does not wear fur in winter. Young people sigh that they are not as good. When lecturing at the conference, he gesticulates with his hands, full of vigor. When he speaks most vigorously, his eyelids open and close non-stop. After inspecting the disaster situation in Hankou and northern Jiangsu, he shook his head whenever he talked about the disaster situation, saying, "It's terrible." Whenever he meets a kind person who donates money for relief, he praises their good deeds, calling them "amazing." Because his colleagues saw that he was a general with a bodhisattva's heart, they all called him the Bodhisattva General. Recently, because he often inspects the disaster situation by plane, he is now also called the Flying General.

Leftover Scraps 177

— (Yin Shouman)

In recent years, various stores have used advertisements of "unprecedented price cuts" to attract customers. Some say that this is actually an ominous phrase, because its homophone is "universal waste and great embarrassment." Now that a great flood has caused disaster, covering seventeen provinces, with more than fifty million refugees, it is a rare disaster in history. This saying has unfortunately come true. After mourning, I can only be dumbfounded.

▲ Correction: In the article "Di Xiangzhai Cheng" reading Pei Jingfu, the handwritten copy incorrectly wrote "min" for "zheng" in "(military and civil administration)". The handwritten copy incorrectly wrote "ju" for "ji" in "(yi Liao strikes the table)". Special correction.

Records of Sights and Sounds of the Old Capital 178

— Zhuan An

Fengtai Peonies

Today, Fengtai is where the Pinghan, Pingsui, and Beining railways intersect. It is the first large station entering Beiping. The south gate of the Jin capital was called Fengyi. The city was abandoned, but the gate site still remains, hence the current name. Every time a train passes through here, if it is during the flowering season, there will be people holding full-bloomed peonies for sale. The red and purple colors are dazzling, making people forget the fatigue of the journey. In the past, the residents of Fengtai all made flower cultivation their business. Continuous irrigation ditches and fields were planted with nothing else. The needs of the inner court and noble families for hair ornaments were so extravagant. The Tang poem says, "Recently, there is no way to deal with the peony. Tens of thousands of coins buy a single clump." The remaining style and charm still exist. Mao Xihe's concubine was named Tiantian, and she was the daughter of a flower seller from this place. She absorbed the wind and drank the dew, and her skin was as fair as a goddess. During the Xianfeng and Tongzhi periods, there were still refined scholars who set up wine here. Wang Renfu's Xiangqilou poetry notes say, "Every year during the flowering season, ten gold pieces must be reserved for one day to prevent them from being cut off, so that they can be appreciated." At that time, it was already considered extravagant. Now, the altars of the soil and grain and the gardens are very prosperous, surrounded by short fences. Walking around for a week, the fragrance fills the sleeves. Few tourists come to Fengtai anymore. The gardening skills of Beiping are the best among the cities. It is difficult to name all the famous flowers and exotic species. What is particularly suitable for the temperament of scholars is the crabapple, in addition to peonies. Generally, families with slightly wider courtyards have two trees. The Zheshuigong Jiangxuexuan, the Nanhai Yinian Hall, and the Yihe Garden Leshou Hall have the most luxuriant plants. My old house in Changsha City had two trees, which were very tall and straight, nearly a hundred years old. They were transplanted from the northern capital by a Manchu named Yu. The firewood and wood were destroyed, and the sacred objects withered. When I moved my family to Beiping, there were also two clumps in the front and back courtyards, one red and one white. Every year, they alternate in prosperity and decline. The white one has twisted branches and casts shade all over the courtyard. Even in Beiping, it is rare. Next are the purple and white lilacs, which grow in clumps, not choosing the location, and bloom before and after the crabapples. The calyxes are small and fragrant. Inserting them in a vase is both elegant and beautiful. Compared to the violets of Europe and America, why are they not as good? Further down are pomegranates and oleanders. These two plants bloom and bear fruit continuously from late spring to mid-autumn. Arranged in the courtyard, they add to the richness. This is also a custom of the old capital. Good people jokingly use two sentences to summarize the situation of Manchu residences: "Awning, fish tank, pomegranate tree, first fatten the dog, then grow the head." The meaning is that the courtyard must have an awning, the door must have a tank to store goldfish, and pomegranates must be decorated in between. "First the dog, then the head" refers to the fact that the owner of the house must first raise a dog and then become an official. Rich and wealthy officials have no elegant bones at all. The arrangement of their homes is gaudy and vulgar, as if vividly seen. Although it is said to be a joke and close to abuse, it cannot be said by those who are not good at understanding things. Every year, as the New Year approaches, the East and West Temple Markets compete to sell Tang flowers, peonies and peach blossoms, planted in pots and basins to reflect the pepper plates, adding color. Cutting paper with scissors seems clumsy. Southern specialties, such as tangerines, pomelos, heavenly candles, jasmine, and Jianlan orchids, are very expensive. If the cultivation is not careful, they will not survive. Almost only wealthy families can grow them. However, those who cultivate them never give up. As for the lotus flowers of Taiye Lake, the colors are the most brilliant. Traveling by car on the Jin'ao and Yudong bridges, in the early sun and cool evening, people enjoy them to their hearts' content. It is not necessary to keep them in the pond. This is something that the south cannot catch up with. Good people like to hold chrysanthemum meetings in the autumn, showing off new and unusual varieties. The five colors are constantly changing. I dislike the fact that it turns elegance into vulgarity, slightly losing the true, leisurely, and natural flavor of Dongli. The same is true of plums in winter. The craftsmen who cultivate plums are difficult to cure of their vulgar bones, and they like to bend the plum branches to fit the model, completely ignoring their horizontal and oblique state. I believe that Beiping's horticulture has a hopeful development, and the livelihood of the citizens depends on it a lot. The municipal authorities should encourage what has already been achieved and guide what is lacking. Everything that is clearly contrary to science and art should be discouraged. The beauty of the four seasons has been described in detail. There is still one thing that I forgot to mention, which is what is commonly called the elm-leaf plum. Its flowers combine the beauty of peach blossoms and crabapples, and it is very easy to grow. It is the "hua e bu ye" of the Tang poem, which is rare in other places, but abundant in the old capital.

The Spinning Wheel Society of Storytellers

A Husband's Wife (8) 179

— Jiang Hongjiao

She never quarreled with her husband, and she never told others her husband's shortcomings completely, so even though she had received such a great stimulus, she still refused to tell Mr. and Mrs. Chen about the woman in the car. She only wept sadly. However, Mr. and Mrs. Chen knew that she was like this because of her husband, but they couldn't say anything in front of Mr. Li.

Mr. Li was very angry in his heart at his wife's narrow-mindedness; at the same time, he complained that Mr. and Mrs. Chen lived in the same house, how could they let her go out in the wind and snow, causing this incident. He thought that no one knew about all his behavior outside, and his wife was naturally kept in the dark, but now he was very worried and very afraid, because his wife had seen through his secret, and he dared not say anything, only quietly smoked cigarettes, sitting on the sofa, waiting for changes, just like enemy troops observing each other's movements, in order to resist. He was considering what kind of strategy to deal with if his wife announced this secret in front of many people. After the police took the thug away, he was a little relieved; Mrs. Li didn't speak, and he was a little relieved again.

"When did she go out? We didn't hear it; the wind and snow outside are so heavy, where did she fall?" Mr. Chen was the first to break the silence in the house and asked, almost starting to attack Mr. Li.

"Today, because the company was checking an account, I didn't finish until two thirty. I hurriedly hired a car to come back, but I didn't expect to see her fall in the snow as soon as I got out of the car. Lan Zhen, why are you so mindless, running out in the middle of the night? You are so silly! I'm not a child, how could I be abducted?" Mr. Li replied to Mr. Chen, and then complained about his wife. Mrs. Li was already very angry in her heart. After hearing her husband's words, she wanted to announce what she had seen, but after a change of mind, she immediately changed her strategy. She felt that if she announced it now, he would definitely be ashamed and angry, and the relationship between the husband and wife might immediately break down and become irreparable. It was better to endure it and make him discover his conscience, realize and turn back. But she was even more depressed and cried so much that she couldn't breathe. Mr. Li wanted to use a gentle method to pretend to comfort his wife; but because he was used to putting on a husband's air, he was suddenly embarrassed to be tender with his wife in front of so many people, so he continued to smoke his cigarettes.

Cotton Market Comparatively Stable 186

The cotton market is stable, and the situation is not yet fully consolidated. Generally speaking, the world situation is not good, and people are still throwing out cotton. However, Han merchants and inland merchants tend to be bullish due to poor harvests. The two sides are holding their ground, and their attitudes are extremely enthusiastic. Transactions of spot cotton are still lacking. Afternoon news from Japanese merchants predicted that the second estimate would be reduced by hundreds of thousands of bales, so the market sentiment was a little tighter. For the time being, it will still hover for a while.

Grain and Rice Market Continues to Fall in Sunny Weather 188

New Early Rice Drops by Half a Yuan... Old Goods Drop by a Small Amount of 3 to 4 Jiao

▲There is Still a Surge in Supply on South City West Road, with Over 30 Arriving Vessels. However, River Sedimentation is Still Thick, and Market Sales are Deserted. In Addition, the Weather is Turning Sunny, and People are Bearish. New Early Round Rice and New Customer Pointed Rice Each Drop by Half a Yuan. Thick Round Rice and Early Rice, Two Varieties, Have Few Enquiries, and Fall by 3 to 4 Jiao. Then, It is Still Difficult to Establish a Foothold. There Are a Small Number of Transactions of Reed Pointed Rice and Foreign Pointed Rice in the Morning. Although the Arrival is Lacking, the Price Continues to Fall by a Jiao. The Situation Still Shows a Slightly Weak Trend. The Thin Rice Market Trends Towards Stability.

▲34 New Vessels Arrive at Xinzha River. The Sales on This Street Are Very Sluggish. The Top Goods of Changzhou and Xizhou Northern Rice Are Sold Wholesale Near the Ruler. Large Merchants are More Peaceful Than South City. Kunshan White Rice Arrives and Sales Are Weak. The Inventory is Not Thick, and the Shop Stomach is Limited. The Price is Still the Original Board. The Market Situation is Extremely Dull. Due to the Fact That Shipu and Chonggu Thin Rice are Not Divided Between Shanghai and Other Cities, Not Many Goods Arrive, and Sales are Also Sluggish. The Market Price Drops by 2 Rulers. New Early Rice in Pudong Continues to Arrive, and Digestion is Not Healthy. The Price Drops by a Small Amount of Half a Yuan. Foreign Rice is Still Softening Due to Unsmooth Sales Channels.

There are Continued Transactions of Road Goods and Saigon Rice 189

Yesterday, Taizhou Customer Indica Rice Saw Slightly Weak Sales on This Street, and the Market Was Soft. There Were No Transactions of White Indica Rice. Rough Rice Still Had a Sales Channel, and 2,500 Bales Were Offered at a Price of 13 Yuan, 12 Yuan and 8 Jiao, and Then Down to 12 Yuan, Which Was Also Slightly Softer Than the Previous Market. Foreign Rice Continuously Has Saigon Rice That Can Arrive, and Customer Sales Are Not Moving. Yesterday, There Was a Small Sale of About 1 Jiao. 1,000 Bales of Spot Goods Were Offered at a Price of 13 Yuan and 4 Jiao and 7 Fen. In Addition, 100 Tons of October Futures Were Offered at a Price of 6 Liang, 5 Qian, and 2.5 Fen. 2,000 Bales of Saigon No. 1 Rice Were Delivered on the 18th at a Price of 14 Yuan and 6 Jiao. There Were Also 500 Tons of Road Goods at a Price of 6 Liang and 9.5 Qian.

The Flour Market Struggles to Escape a Weak Situation 190

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, the market situation for each month still trended towards a weak and tired state. This is because the bullish side seems to have been discouraged since the government decided to use foreign wheat for disaster relief and cannot raise prices. In addition, the sales of Russian wheat are still frequently inquired about, and it seems that one wave has not subsided, and another wave is rising. Surplus food from abroad is fiercely entering China, so most people's hearts are dim. After observing the future steps, it should show a long-term tired and short-term smart situation. As a result, this month fell by 1 fen compared to the previous day, October and November fell by 1 fen, December fell by 1 fen and 2 li, and January and February fell by 7 li and 5 hao.

The Wheat Market Is Tired and Languid 191

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat market in the morning and afternoon, the market situation for each month again showed a state of fatigue and stagnation. This is because although there are no quotations for foreign wheat, the hearts of the inland merchants are that the chips in the market are expanding like this, and in addition, the sales of Russian wheat are rampant in the market with rumors that they only need between 3 Liang, 6 Qian, and 7 Qian. Although the goods are inferior to European and American wheat, they are much higher than Chinese wheat, so people's hearts continue to soften, and future steps are still difficult to reset. As a result, this month fell by 2 fen compared to the previous day, October fell by 3 fen, November fell by 2 fen, December fell by 1 fen, January fell by 2 fen, and February improved by 1 fen. Spot wheat saw quiet transactions and no business was done.

The Demand for Five Fortune White Crystal Sugar Exceeds Supply 192

Each Mound Rises by Another 2 Qian

The Five Fortune White Crystal Sugar Xiamen Factory has been cooking for many days, but because it cannot be dried due to rain, it could not be transported to Shanghai in the early stage. Yesterday, the Jinan Ship of Taikoo Company finally transported a batch of more than 100 boxes. Upon hearing the news, various firms rushed to buy them, resulting in the price of each mound rising by another 2 Qian. It opened at 9 Liang and 4 Qian, which was not enough to distribute. The firmness surpassed Heng. Dongxian's Xitaiyuan Sand has been in short supply for a long time, and the upper grade is lacking. Although other brands of goods have declined, they are not liked by customers and are difficult to price.

Domestically Produced Jian Crystal Sugar Opens Extremely Smartly 193

Sales of Waste Raw Sugar Gradually Occur

Yesterday, the sugar market production area telegraphed that there were few arrivals in Cuba and New York. The current and future prices of Java sugar were unchanged compared to the previous day. The association market allocated the board. Transactions of Dutch Sugar No. 24 Waste Raw Sugar White were scarce, and the transaction price was still 11 Liang and 7 Qian. No. 20 Medium Sugar White Was 11 Liang and 2 Qian. The Market Situation is Still Increasing. Taikoo Sugar is Imported and Exported Very Prosperously. Door-to-Door Delivery is Extremely Lacking. HM-Mark is 11 Liang, 4 Qian to 4 Qian and 2.5 Fen. HX-Mark is 11 Liang, 7 Qian to 7 Qian and 5 Fen. The Market Conditions Are All Firm and Smart. Silk and Tea Factories' American Sales Are Unsustained 194

Yesterday, the silk market of foreign firms in this port still trended towards quiet tiredness. This is because the New York market was affected by economic instability, and the price of silk was reported to have fallen. The telegram transfer was stagnant, and the European firm sales stomach was also good. Yesterday, only Lanye Bi and others bought 70 bales of Shanghai White Factory Handled Silk, and Dada and others bought 20 bales of White Dry Handled Silk. The price was still stable.

Rice Cocoons and Italian Silk Sales are Stagnant and Prices Fall 195

European and American Silk Telegrams Are Not Transferred... Prices Fall by 4 to 5 Lire

The Rice Cocoon Market, Recently, the Italian silk market has turned tired and stagnant. This is because silk sales in New York have stopped again. British and French silk telegrams are also rarely transferred, and silk prices have been reported to have fallen. On Monday, the price of each kilo of Double Special Grade was only 391 lire, Special Grade was 343 lire, and Superior Grade was 287 lire, each falling by 4 to 5 lire.

Needle Eyebrow Green Tea Sales to Europe Turn Smooth 196

Yesterday, the needle eyebrow green tea from Lailu Zhuang, British firms such as Yihua, Xiehe, Jinlong, and Tongfu, etc., showed increasing interest, and the entire city traded more than 1,000 boxes. The top board opened to 82 Liang, which was 3 to 4 Liang higher than before. The market for Zhenmei and Gongxi items was also quite firm, but transactions were slightly quieter than before. Currently, the source of supply from all roads has been cut off, and the inventory is thin. The market seems to be unaffected.

The Price of New Lead Wire in the Hardware Market Rises by 2.5 Qian 197

Hardware transactions are extremely deserted because customer sales are stagnant and tired. The market conditions in each city are also almost unremarkable. However, because there is less stock of No. 16 to No. 20 new lead wire, the price rose by 2.5 Qian yesterday, estimated at 13 Liang and 2.5 Qian per dan, and No. 21 to No. 25 was 18 Liang and 7 Qian and 5 Fen. It is heard that more than 600 to 700 dan were offered, but the inventory is becoming more and more scarce, and people's hearts are more determined. If there are no arrivals within one or two weeks, the market price may rise again.

20th Year Jiangsu Province County Road Construction Plan 217

— Ming

Zhenjiang Correspondence: The Jiangsu Construction Bureau, in order to rectify the road construction methods of various counties, recently convened a joint meeting of the heads of construction bureaus from various counties in batches. An overall plan was formulated to facilitate collaborative efforts and achieve twice the results with half the effort. A total of seven meetings were held, and the sections and dates of the 20th-year road construction plans for various counties were fully discussed. These are detailed below:

▲ First Meeting: Attendees included over ten construction bureau chiefs and technicians from Zhenjiang, Danyang, Jintan, Gaochun, Lishui, Jurong, Jiangning, and Yangzhong counties. Resolutions: (1) The entire Zhen-Guang Road from Zhenjiang to Jintan will be completed within eight months. The section from Jintan to Liyang will have culverts and temporary bridges built, or existing bridges will be used to allow light vehicles to pass. (2) For the Li-Ning Road, the entire road surface project from Lishui to Jing (Nanjing) will be completed within this year. The bureau will allocate construction bonds for subsidies and send personnel to assist. (3) The entire Danyang Ring Road project will be completed. For the Jintan Ring Road, one bridge will be built first. (4) Other roads where bridges should be built first for traffic are listed below: (1) Lishui to Gaochun. (2) Lishui to Liyang (Jing-Hang Road), Shangxingbu. (3) Dan-Ju Road. (4) Ju-Shu Road. (5) After the completion of the earthen roads this year, a trial implementation of labor requisition for road maintenance will be conducted. (6) The construction bureaus of each county should re-draft the annual budget according to the above regulations. If there is a shortage of funds, a proposal for raising funds should be submitted to the bureau for approval. (7) The date for labor requisition for road construction in the eight counties under Nanjing's jurisdiction is set for preparation within October, and construction must start no later than December 1st.

▲ Second Meeting: Attendees included construction bureau chiefs from Wu County, Wujiang, Jiangyin, Wuxi, Wujin, Yixing, and other counties. Resolutions: (1) The entire section of the Huanhu (Ring Lake) Road from Yixing to Wuxi will be completed within this year. (2) The entire section of the Huanhu Road from Yixing to Wuxi will have bridges, culverts, and earthen roads built for traffic this year, up to Beitan Town in Wujiang County. (3) The entire Xi-Chang (Wuxi-Changzhou) to Tai-Chang (Taicang-Changshu) provincial highway will be completed within this year. (4) Jiangyin will complete the entire Cheng-Xi (Jiangyin City-Wuxi) Road within its borders. Depending on financial resources, it will proceed towards Zhonggang Town. (5) From Wujin to Caoqiao, Wujin to Benniu, and from Benniu to Yinshakou, all bridges and culverts will be completed. A cinder road will be paved for traffic. (6) The funds required for the above road construction plan, in addition to the surplus mu tax from the 19th year and the newly collected amount in the 20th year allocated for this purpose, will be raised through the following methods if there is a shortfall: 1. Borrowing funds locally, using the 21st year mu tax as collateral. 2. The bureau will allocate construction bonds to supplement the Huanhu Road expenses. 3. Borrowing funds from the automobile company, using vehicle tax as collateral.

▲ Third Meeting: Attendees included construction bureau chiefs and technicians from Jiangdu, Liuhe, Jiangpu, Taixing, Jingjiang, and other counties. Resolutions: (1) The following roads should be fully completed: 1. The Jiangdu to Chenjiagou section of the Yang-You Road and the Yang-Huo Road. 2. The Xinghua to Kou'an section of the Yu-Yang-You Road and the Yu-Long Road. 3. The extension of the Jiang-Jing Road, the Jingxie section, and the ring road of Jingjiang. 4. Huangqiao via Lijia City to Jingjiang. 5. The Yi-Si section. (2) The following roads will have completed bridges, culverts, and earthen roads for traffic: 1. The He-Pu Road and Pu-Wu Road. 2. The Yang-Yi Road. 3. The Shaobo to Yuluzhen section of the Yang-You Road. (3) Each construction bureau should re-draft the annual budget according to the above regulations and send it to the bureau for review. If there is a shortage of funds, the proposed fundraising methods should also be submitted to the bureau for reference.

▲ Fourth Meeting: Attendees included construction bureau chiefs and technicians from Tongshan, Peixian, Dangshan, Xiaoxian, Suqian, Pixian, and other counties. Resolutions: (1) The entire Tong-Xiao Road project will be completed. (2) The following roads will have completed bridges, culverts, and earthen roads for traffic: 1. The Dang-Feng Road. 2. The Fan-Shan Road. 3. The Pei-Feng Road. 4. The Pei-Tong Road. 5. The Tong-Sui section of the Gua-Yu provincial highway. 6. The Su-Sui Road. 7. The Su-Yang Road. 8. The Pi-Su section of the Pi-Si provincial highway. (3) Organize the old roads to facilitate traffic: 1. The Su-Su section. 2. The Pi-Shou section. 3. The Guan-Yun section. 4. The Pao-Mao section. 5. The Pi-Tan section.

▲ Fifth Meeting: Attendees included construction bureau chiefs from Shanghai, Baoshan, Jiading, Taicang, Fengxian, Kunshan, Qingpu, Songjiang, Jinshan, Nanhui, Chuansha, and other counties. Resolutions: (1) Roads with complete projects: 1. Kun-Tai Road. 2. Kunshan County town to the train station road. 3. Tai-Jia section. 4. Jiading connecting line. 5. Tai-Chang section. 6. Songjiang to Beiqiao Town. 7. Connect Yi-Chuan-Chuan-Qin Road. 8. Baoshan to Yuepu section. 9. Nanzhao to Beiqiao Town connected. 10. Qingpu to Hongqiao. 11. Xin-Zhou Section. (2) Roads passable for earthen roads: 1. Zhu-Qing section. 2. Jinshan to Songjiang. 3. Songjiang Jingsi connects Qingpu. 4. Nanzhao via Zhaolin, along the pond, passing through Songjiang into Jinshan County, reaching Zhejiang to connect with Zhejiang (If unable to complete this year, rebuild Nanzhao to Zhuanghang). 5. Chuan-Nan Road. 6. Nan-Xin Section.

▲ Sixth Meeting: Attendees included construction bureau chiefs from Nantong, Haimen, Qidong, Chongming, Rugao, and other counties. Resolutions: (1) Nantong should complete the entire project of the Cheng-Yao Road ring road and the section from Pingchao to Rugao border (Dong-Chu provincial highway). The Yun-Gang Road should have completed bridges, culverts, and earthen roads for traffic. (2) Rugao should complete the road surface project of the Tong-Yu provincial highway's Tong-Ru section and the connecting section of the Ru-Li Road and Longyou Road. Various roads such as the Dingfenshan section of the Ru-Kan Road or its extension to Matang Town should have completed bridges, culverts, and earthen roads for traffic. (3) Haimen should complete the Xing-Hong Road, Lingjiang Road, Mao-Zhao Road, and the section of the Tong-Yu provincial highway extending eastward from Haimen to Tangjia Town with completed bridges, culverts, and earthen roads for traffic. (4) Chongming's Chong-Xi Road, from Chongming County town to the Caohong line point, and from Chongming County town to Bang Town or extended to Xinkaihe, Beibao Town to Xianghua Town, should have completed bridges, culverts, and earthen roads for traffic. (5) Qidong's section from Nanqing River to Gongsi Town should have completed bridge and culvert projects and earthen roads for traffic. (6) The development of earthen roads in various counties within this region is quite advanced. To ensure rapid maintenance, it is proposed to purchase small road maintenance machinery for trial use.

Ford Mobile Cinema 218

The above image shows a movie screen within a picture. It is a tool for Ford Motor Company's educational work in China. The projector and generator are installed in a new Ford delivery truck's panel body. It can travel to various places with a portable screen. The floodlight installed on top of the panel body is used to illuminate the cinema area during evening screenings.

This equipment will be unveiled at the opening of the Road Exhibition in Shanghai (September 12th to October 2nd). After the exhibition closes, it will be transported to various parts of China. Screenings can be held even in places without electricity. The films shown will be various Ford educational films. The dialogue in the sound films will be in Mandarin Chinese. The generator is currently on display at Meitong Motors for viewing.

The Trend of Automobile Progress 219

— Gan

Since the invention of the automobile, only a few decades have passed, yet it has swept the globe, serving humanity and being regarded as the only convenient means of transportation in modern times. Moreover, automobile manufacturers and renowned mechanical inventors in Europe and America have spared no effort in meticulously researching to make the application of automobiles perfect. Therefore, since the first automobile came into the world, the various reforms and advancements in the past few decades are too numerous to mention. The motivations behind these can be roughly summarized into three aspects: 1. Striving for precision in the mechanical aspect, to increase efficiency during use, add speed, and ensure stable operation. This is the most important aspect. 2. Achieving mass production to reduce costs, lower prices, and facilitate widespread sales for broad distribution. 3. Changing various styles and colors to meet the needs of society and achieve aesthetic appeal. While these three aspects may not encompass all the reasons for the progress of automobiles, they are the most significant and are not far from the truth.

In terms of modern commercial trends, the first question after a product is created is how to sell it as much as possible. However, to achieve high sales, it must start with needs. For example, after an automobile is manufactured, if the public has no need for it, then there is no doubt that the automobile cannot be sold. On the other hand, the purchasing public may not yet know what they need, which is also a common phenomenon. However, while what is needed may not be clear, what is not needed is well-known and self-evident without explanation. Let's take an example to prove that this statement is not wrong. Suppose a certain automobile factory manufactures a new car where the engine start and brakes are all controlled by a single button, which is convenient and unprecedented. This innovation is certainly needed by the public, but before this car is launched, the public may not have had such a need. This is not accidental. Conversely, if there is another automobile with a bulky body and slow movement, then the purchasing public will retreat without even asking about it. Why? Because it is not needed.

Several years ago, the production volume of automobiles was not as high as in recent years. The colors of the car bodies were extremely monotonous, with only one color. The commonly used color was black, which was simple, dull, and lacked liveliness. However, car users at that time were accustomed to it and did not feel uncomfortable. The reason for this was probably that the speed and stability of automobiles at that time had not yet reached a perfect state. There were many aspects of the machinery that needed innovation and research, so the aesthetics of car body colors were not yet a priority. Today, with many improvements and innovations in the mechanical aspects, the public's need for beautifying automobiles is evident. Therefore, the colors of car bodies are coordinated and adjusted to strive for beauty, lightness, elegance, and vibrancy. If you visit various car factories, you will find that the new cars they produce mostly have various colors, allowing customers to choose. They can also customize the color according to the customer's preferences. The progress of automobiles has reached maturity.

Now, let's talk about the cylinder issue of the automobile itself. In the past, automobiles mostly had four cylinders. Later, due to the public's need for speed and stability, six-cylinder automobiles emerged. Today, in addition to six cylinders, eight cylinders or even more are needed. The cylinders have a great relationship with the automobile's operation. When car factories switched from four-cylinder cars to six-cylinder cars, they spent tens of millions of dollars to renovate factories and machinery. Now, if they want to upgrade from six cylinders to eight cylinders, the amount of money spent will be even greater. In summary, although this kind of improvement is in response to the trend of the times, the main point is still due to the eager demand of the purchasers. As there are many cars produced by each factory and the competition is fierce, they do not hesitate to spend tens of millions of dollars to solve these pressing problems.

Finally, there is the issue of the automobile's selling price. Once a car is made, it must be sold to the buyer. How to attract the attention of customers and achieve the purpose of sales is also worth studying. Various additional expenses will also arise. Therefore, in addition to the cost of the car body, a certain amount of sales expenses must be added. As for the various uses of the factory, these are necessary expenses. Even if the car is not sold, these expenses continue to arise and cannot be stopped, just as a cow needs fodder even if it is not plowing. Based on the above reasons, the issue of the automobile's selling price is a crucial matter for each car factory. In the past, when production was low and labor was expensive, the selling price was very high compared to now. Today, most factories adopt the policy of mass production and strive to reduce labor costs while increasing productivity. Therefore, the quality of the goods is better than before, while the price has fallen.
